      <div class="post-176473 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-international-politicsculture-stuff category-musicentlit category-nz-politicsculturestuff tag-reddit-revolt" id="post-176473">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/reddits-fate-hangs-in-the-balance-as-revolt-against-ceo-makes-waves/" rel="bookmark">
         Reddits fate hangs in the balance as revolt against CEO makes waves..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/reddits-fate-hangs-in-the-balance-as-revolt-against-ceo-makes-waves/" rel="bookmark" title="7:40 am">
         <span class="entry-date">
          8/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/technology/2015/jul/07/reddit-revolt-ellen-pao-fate" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/technology/2015/jul/07/reddit-revolt-ellen-pao-fate', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://static.guim.co.uk/sys-images/Guardian/Pix/pictures/2015/7/7/1436290611808/18330449416_722de8361c_o-2060x1236.jpeg"/>
          </a>
          While more than 200,000 Redditors want Ellen Pao to resign  readers are jumping ship to budding competitor sites  as top brass pushes to go mainstream.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="auto-linked-tag" data-link-name="auto-linked-tag" href="http://www.theguardian.com/technology/reddit" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/technology/reddit', 'Reddit ');">
           Reddit 
          </a>
          the giant online discussion forum for everyone from political junkies to billiards enthusiasts  is in revolt.
         </p>
         <p>
          Over 10 years, Reddit  which styles itself as the front page of the internet has built a site that attracts 164 million readers a month. Last week however its users mounted an open insurrection against the California-based companys interim CEO, Ellen Pao  following what they say have been a series of unpopular decisions by management that directly contradict the open democratic style of discussion that Reddit has previously encouraged. And despite the company issuing an apology on the site on Monday a petition calling for Pao to step down now boasts more than
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="in-body-link" data-link-name="in body link" href="https://www.change.org/p/ellen-k-pao-step-down-as-ceo-of-reddit-inc" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'https://www.change.org/p/ellen-k-pao-step-down-as-ceo-of-reddit-inc', '200,000 signatures');">
           200,000 signatures
          </a>
          .
         </p>
         <aside class="element element-rich-link element--thumbnail element-rich-link--upgraded" data-component="rich-link" data-link-name="rich-link-2 | 1">
          <div class="rich-link tone-news--item ">
           <div class="rich-link__container">
            <div class="rich-link__image-container u-responsive-ratio">
             <img alt="" src="http://i.guim.co.uk/static/w-460/h--/q-95/sys-images/Guardian/Pix/pictures/2015/7/4/1436018118018/2b62c53f-2222-44d9-b92f-7b9df6d00736-460x276.jpeg"/>
            </div>
            <div class="rich-link__image-container u-responsive-ratio">
            </div>
            <div class="rich-link__image-container u-responsive-ratio">
             Redditors  as users are called  have accused the site of increasingly trying to monetize its popularity and it appears their sentiments came to a head last Thursday when Reddits popular director of talent Victoria Taylor was
             <a class=" u-underline" data-component="in-body-link" data-link-name="in body link" href="https://www.reddit.com/r/OutOfTheLoop/comments/3bw39q/why_has_riama_been_set_to_private/csq204d" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'https://www.reddit.com/r/OutOfTheLoop/comments/3bw39q/why_has_riama_been_set_to_private/csq204d', 'let go from her post');">
              let go from her post
             </a>
             .
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="rich-link__image-container u-responsive-ratio">
           </div>
           <div class="rich-link__image-container u-responsive-ratio">
            (cont..)
           </div>
           <div class="rich-link__container">
            <div class="rich-link__image-container u-responsive-ratio">
            </div>
            <div class="rich-link__header">
             <p>
              Source:
              <em>
               <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/technology/2015/jul/07/reddit-revolt-ellen-pao-fate" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/technology/2015/jul/07/reddit-revolt-ellen-pao-fate', 'Reddits fate hangs in the balance as revolt against CEO makes waves | Technology | The Guardian');">
                Reddits fate hangs in the balance as revolt against CEO makes waves | Technology | The Guardian
               </a>
              </em>
             </p>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
         </aside>
        </blockquote>

      <div class="post-176471 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-international-politicsculture-stuff category-nz-politicsculturestuff tag-encryption tag-spooks" id="post-176471">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/uk-and-us-demands-to-access-encrypted-data-are-unprincipled-and-unworkable/" rel="bookmark">
         UK and US demands to access encrypted data are unprincipled and unworkable..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/uk-and-us-demands-to-access-encrypted-data-are-unprincipled-and-unworkable/" rel="bookmark" title="7:01 am">
         <span class="entry-date">
          8/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2015/jul/07/uk-and-us-demands-to-access-encrypted-data-are-unprincipled-and-unworkable" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/world/2015/jul/07/uk-and-us-demands-to-access-encrypted-data-are-unprincipled-and-unworkable', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://media.guim.co.uk/92adaffea0ea0aeace44e3bdbd8c6ab897987f53/0_92_3000_1799/master/3000.jpg"/>
          </a>
          Influential group of international cryptographers and computer scientists says proposals will open door to criminals and malicious nation states.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          Demands by US and British security agencies for access to encrypted communication data have been dealt a serious blow in a report by an influential group of cryptographers and computer scientists who dismiss the move as unprincipled and unworkable.
         </p>
         <p>
          They warn that such access will open doors through which criminals and malicious nation states can attack the very individuals law enforcement seeks to defend.
         </p>
         <p>
          The report says: The costs would be substantial  the damage to innovation severe and the consequences for economic growth hard to predict. The costs to our moral authority would also be considerable.
         </p>
         <p>
          The expert opinion comes on the eve of an appearance before the US Senate intelligence committee by the FBI director, James Comey  who last year savaged tech companies for embracing end-to-end encryption  claiming it would deprive the security services of potentially life-saving information.
         </p>
         <p>
          David Cameron and the home secretary Theresa May are proposing to introduce legislation in the autumn to force companies such as Apple Google and Microsoft to provide access to encrypted data. The proposed legislation has been requested by the intelligence agencies  which say encryption has made their job much more difficult.
         </p>
         <p>
          (cont..)
         </p>
         <p>
          Source:
          <em>
           <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2015/jul/07/uk-and-us-demands-to-access-encrypted-data-are-unprincipled-and-unworkable" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/world/2015/jul/07/uk-and-us-demands-to-access-encrypted-data-are-unprincipled-and-unworkable', 'UK and US demands to access encrypted data are unprincipled and unworkable | World news | The Guardian');">
            UK and US demands to access encrypted data are unprincipled and unworkable | World news | The Guardian
           </a>
          </em>
         </p>
        </blockquote>

             <a class="share-google-plus-1 sd-button share-icon" data-shared="sharing-google-176471" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/uk-and-us-demands-to-access-encrypted-data-are-unprincipled-and-unworkable/?share=google-plus-1" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="Click to share on Google+">
              <span>
               Google
              </span>
             </a>
            </li>
            <li class="share-end">
            </li>
           </ul>
          </div>
         </div>

      <div class="post-176469 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-international-politicsculture-stuff tag-germany tag-greek-crisis" id="post-176469">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/greeces-lenders-who-has-most-to-lose/" rel="bookmark">
         Greeces lenders: who has most to lose?..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/greeces-lenders-who-has-most-to-lose/" rel="bookmark" title="6:50 am">
         <span class="entry-date">
          8/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/business/2015/jul/07/greeces-lenders-who-has-the-most-to-lose" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/business/2015/jul/07/greeces-lenders-who-has-the-most-to-lose', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://i.guim.co.uk/img/static/sys-images/Guardian/Pix/pictures/2015/7/7/1436272878834/436b5b45-7604-42d4-8994-f956e4290a93-620x291.png?w=620&amp;q=85&amp;auto=format&amp;sharp=10&amp;s=a7fb389cd02a31e19602f9ba4cd129f2"/>
          </a>
          Exposure to Greek loans is weighing heavily on minds in the eurozone  in Spain  Slovenia and Malta perhaps more than Germany.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          As eurozone leaders meet in another effort to broker a deal between
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="auto-linked-tag" data-link-name="auto-linked-tag" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/greece" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/world/greece', 'Greece');">
           Greece
          </a>
          and its creditors  those who have lent to the near-bankrupt country are asking if they will ever get their money back.
         </p>
         <p>
          Greece owes 323bn (228bn) to a combination of official and private creditors  equivalent to more than 175% of its GDP. Much of that debt mountain was built up by Greece receiving bailout packages  funded in part by its eurozone neighbours.
         </p>
         <p>
          Germany is far and away the most exposed country within the single currency bloc. However, when adjusting exposure for the sizes of a countrys respective economy 
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="auto-linked-tag" data-link-name="auto-linked-tag" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/germany" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/world/germany', 'Germany');">
           Germany
          </a>
          appears better placed than most neighbours to absorb losses.
         </p>
         <aside class="element element-rich-link element--thumbnail element-rich-link--upgraded" data-component="rich-link" data-link-name="rich-link-1 | 1">
          <div class="rich-link tone-news--item ">
           <div class="rich-link__container">
            <div class="rich-link__image-container u-responsive-ratio">
             <img alt="" src="http://i.guim.co.uk/media/w-460/h--/q-95/e2c80d2aeaa25a47990277fb8304bed57050c45c/0_0_4928_2957/500.jpg"/>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
         </aside>
         <p>
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="auto-linked-tag" data-link-name="auto-linked-tag" href="http://www.theguardian.com/business/eurozone" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/business/eurozone', 'Eurozone');">
           Eurozone
          </a>
          governments loaned Greece 52.9bn under the first bailout in 2010 and a further 141.8bn under a bailout in 2012.
         </p>
         <p>
          Germanys exposure for the two bailouts is 57.23bn- with Franceowed 42.98bn  Italyowed 37.76bn and Spain 25.1bn  according to
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="in-body-link" data-link-name="in body link" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2015/06/28/us-eurozone-greece-debt-factbox-idUSKCN0P80XW20150628" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.reuters.com/article/2015/06/28/us-eurozone-greece-debt-factbox-idUSKCN0P80XW20150628', 'calculations by Reuters');">
           calculations by Reuters
          </a>
          based on official data. That is in addition to those countries contributions to International Monetary Fund (IMF) loans made to Greece.
         </p>
         <p>
          When taking into account the countries exposure via bailouts  via
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="auto-linked-tag" data-link-name="auto-linked-tag" href="http://www.theguardian.com/business/european-central-bank" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/business/european-central-bank', 'European Central Bank');">
           European Central Bank
          </a>
          (ECB) loans and via their banking systems  Germany is again well out in front  according to the thinktank Open Europe.
         </p>
         <p>
          (cont..)
         </p>
         <p>
          Source:
          <em>
           <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/business/2015/jul/07/greeces-lenders-who-has-the-most-to-lose" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/business/2015/jul/07/greeces-lenders-who-has-the-most-to-lose', 'Greeces lenders: who has most to lose? | Business | The Guardian');">
            Greeces lenders: who has most to lose? | Business | The Guardian
           </a>
          </em>
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <div class="sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled">

      <!-- #post-## -->
      <div class="post-176466 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-international-politicsculture-stuff tag-greek-crisis" id="post-176466">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/bryan-gould-eu-power-brokers-have-guilty-role-in-greek-tragedy/" rel="bookmark">
         Bryan Gould: EU power brokers have guilty role in Greek tragedy..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/bryan-gould-eu-power-brokers-have-guilty-role-in-greek-tragedy/" rel="bookmark" title="6:41 am">
         <span class="entry-date">
          8/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.nzherald.co.nz/opinion/news/article.cfm?c_id=466&amp;objectid=11476648" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.nzherald.co.nz/opinion/news/article.cfm?c_id=466&amp;objectid=11476648', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://media.nzherald.co.nz/webcontent/image/jpg/201528/SCCZEN_AP150628164206_1024x768.jpg"/>
          </a>
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          Most people will feel they dont need to look far for an explanation as to what lies behind the Greek crisis. Lazy reporting and racial stereotyping will persuade them the Greeks have spent more than they should  got into debt  taken out loans from the hard-working Germans and now wont repay the loans because they refuse to tighten their belts.
         </p>
         <p>
          But another narrative tells a somewhat different story  one of a powerful economy enforcing its will on its weaker neighbours and refusing to acknowledge it has thereby made it impossible for them to dig themselves out of a hole.
         </p>
         <figure class="inlineMedia inlineMedia-inline-video inlineMedia-left inlineMedia-width620">
          <a class="inlineModal fancybox.ajax imgWrap" href="http://www.nzherald.co.nz/opinion/news/video.cfm?c_id=466&amp;gallery_id=152120&amp;gal_objectid=11476648" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.nzherald.co.nz/opinion/news/video.cfm?c_id=466&amp;gallery_id=152120&amp;gal_objectid=11476648', '  Video ');">
           <img alt="" src="http://media.nzherald.co.nz/webcontent/image/jpg/201528/eco_620x310.jpg"/>
           <span class="vidOver">
            Video
           </span>
          </a>
         </figure>
         <p>
          The story begins in 2000 when the Greeks  along with many others  were persuaded that being part of Europe required them to give up their own currency and accept the euro. A single currency meant a single monetary policy and a single central bank- and guess who decided what that policy should be and what the central bank should do?
         </p>
         <div class="advert" id="DivContentRect">
          Germany- by far the most powerful economy in the eurozone  ran it to serve its own interests but life wasnt so easy for the weaker countries. The Greeks for example with their smaller and less developed economy, had no chance of surviving the competition from efficient German manufacturing.
         </div>
         <div class="advert">
         </div>
         <div class="advert">
          We dont need hindsight to make this point as many commentators  myself included  foresaw this inevitable outcome at the time.
         </div>
         <div class="advert">
         </div>
         <div class="advert">
          (cont..)
         </div>
         <div class="advert">
         </div>
         <div class="advert">
          Source:
          <em>
           <a href="http://www.nzherald.co.nz/business/news/article.cfm?c_id=3&amp;objectid=11476648" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.nzherald.co.nz/business/news/article.cfm?c_id=3&amp;objectid=11476648', 'Bryan Gould: EU power brokers have guilty role in Greek tragedy  Opinion  NZ Herald News');">
            Bryan Gould: EU power brokers have guilty role in Greek tragedy  Opinion  NZ Herald News
           </a>
          </em>
         </div>
        </blockquote>
        <div class="sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled">

      <!-- #post-## -->
      <div class="post-176464 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-green-things category-international-politicsculture-stuff category-nz-politicsculturestuff tag-greenhouse-gas-emissions" id="post-176464">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/critics-slam-govt-goal-on-greenhouse-gas-cutback/" rel="bookmark">
         Critics slam Govt goal on greenhouse gas cutback..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/critics-slam-govt-goal-on-greenhouse-gas-cutback/" rel="bookmark" title="6:18 am">
         <span class="entry-date">
          8/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.nzherald.co.nz/nz/news/article.cfm?c_id=1&amp;objectid=11477172" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.nzherald.co.nz/nz/news/article.cfm?c_id=1&amp;objectid=11477172', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://media.nzherald.co.nz/webcontent/image/jpg/201528/SCCZEN_A_NZPA68861_300x200.jpg"/>
          </a>
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          The Government has set what is says is an achievable fair target for cutting atmosphere-warming emissions  but critics say the new target is 100 per cent pure spin and a paltry increase on past commitments.
         </p>
         <p>
          All countries are expected to set new targets for reducing greenhouse gas emissions before crucial climate change talks in Paris in December  which will establish a road map for the period after 2020.
         </p>
         <p>
          Minister for Climate Change Issues Tim Groser confirmed yesterday New Zealands target would be to reduce greenhouse gas emissions by 30 per cent from 2005 levels by 2030.
         </p>
         <p>
          He described it as a significant increase on the 2020 target  which was a reduction of 5 per cent below 1990 levels. If the new target was set to a 1990 baseline  it was the equivalent of an 11 per cent reduction.
         </p>
         <p>
          Labour and the Greens slammed the target  saying the Government should match the European Union by setting a target of at least a 40 per cent reduction on 1990 levels.
         </p>
         <div class="advert" id="DivContentRect">
          Green Party spokesman Kennedy Graham said using 2005 as a benchmark was pure spin. Once the usual benchmark of 1990 was considered, the reduction was paltry  he said.
         </div>
         <div class="advert">
         </div>
         <div class="advert">
          (cont..)
         </div>
         <div class="advert">
         </div>
         <div class="advert">
          Source:
          <em>
           <a href="http://www.nzherald.co.nz/nz/news/article.cfm?c_id=1&amp;objectid=11477172" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.nzherald.co.nz/nz/news/article.cfm?c_id=1&amp;objectid=11477172', 'Critics slam Govt goal on greenhouse gas cutback  National  NZ Herald News');">
            Critics slam Govt goal on greenhouse gas cutback  National  NZ Herald News
           </a>
          </em>
         </div>
        </blockquote>
        <div class="sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled">
         <div class="robots-nocontent sd-block sd-social sd-social-icon-text sd-sharing">

              <span>

              </span>

      <div class="post-176462 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-nz-politicsculturestuff tag-christchurch tag-uber" id="post-176462">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/more-than-1300-apply-for-uber-jobs-in-christchurch/" rel="bookmark">
         More than 1300 apply for Uber jobs in Christchurch..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/more-than-1300-apply-for-uber-jobs-in-christchurch/" rel="bookmark" title="5:53 am">
         <span class="entry-date">
          8/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.stuff.co.nz/business/industries/69860638/more-than-1300-apply-for-uber-jobs-in-christchurch" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.stuff.co.nz/business/industries/69860638/more-than-1300-apply-for-uber-jobs-in-christchurch', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://www.stuff.co.nz/content/dam/images/1/5/p/2/b/1/image.related.StuffLandscapeSixteenByNine.620x349.15lcta.png/1436260057526.jpg"/>
          </a>
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          More than 1300 people have applied to be Uber drivers in Christchurch.
         </p>
         <p>
          The rideshare company has yet to set a launch date for the Garden City  the third centre to get it after Auckland and Wellington.
         </p>
         <p>
          Uberconnects people who need a ride with adriverthrough a smartphone app. It allows everyday people to make money by
          <a href="http://www.stuff.co.nz/motoring/69090386/government-says-it-will-take-the-lightest-touch-possible-to-regulating-uber" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.stuff.co.nz/motoring/69090386/government-says-it-will-take-the-lightest-touch-possible-to-regulating-uber', 'driving others around in their own cars');" target="_blank">
           <b>
            driving others around in their own cars
           </b>
          </a>
          .
         </p>
         <p>
          Uber  which operates in 58 countries  has more than1000driversinAucklandandWellington after launching in 2014
         </p>
         <p>
          Its establishment in Christchurch will come after the
          <a href="http://www.stuff.co.nz/business/industries/65226952/Government-to-review-taxi-rules-after-Uber-campaign" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.stuff.co.nz/business/industries/65226952/Government-to-review-taxi-rules-after-Uber-campaign', 'Governments review of small passenger services ');" target="_blank">
           <b>
            Governments review of small passenger services 
           </b>
          </a>
          the results of whichare due later this year.
         </p>
         <p>
          In May Uber representatives scouted for driversat Christchurchs Northlands Shopping Centre.
         </p>
         <p>
          Uber New Zealands general manager Oscar Peppitt said the company had received more than 1300 applications to be a driver partner in Christchurch in the past few months.
         </p>
         <p>
          (cont..)
         </p>
         <p>
          Source:
          <em>
           <a href="http://www.stuff.co.nz/business/industries/69860638/more-than-1300-apply-for-uber-jobs-in-christchurch" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.stuff.co.nz/business/industries/69860638/more-than-1300-apply-for-uber-jobs-in-christchurch', 'More than 1300 apply for Uber jobs in Christchurch | Stuff.co.nz');">
            More than 1300 apply for Uber jobs in Christchurch | Stuff.co.nz
           </a>
          </em>
         </p>
        </blockquote>

      <div class="post-176460 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-international-politicsculture-stuff tag-bernie-sanders" id="post-176460">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/bernie-sanders-on-why-elites-are-in-for-a-shock-the-discontent-of-the-american-people-is-far-far-greater/" rel="bookmark">
         Bernie Sanders on why elites are in for a shock: The discontent of the American people is far far greater..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/bernie-sanders-on-why-elites-are-in-for-a-shock-the-discontent-of-the-american-people-is-far-far-greater/" rel="bookmark" title="9:06 pm">
         <span class="entry-date">
          7/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.salon.com/2015/07/06/bernie_sanders_on_why_elites_are_in_for_a_shock_the_discontent_of_the_american_people_is_far_far_greater/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.salon.com/2015/07/06/bernie_sanders_on_why_elites_are_in_for_a_shock_the_discontent_of_the_american_people_is_far_far_greater/', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://media.salon.com/2014/09/bernie_sanders3.jpg"/>
          </a>
          The chattering class doesnt see it yet  but America is ripe for a political revolution  Sanders tells The Nation.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          In a new wide-ranging interview with
          <a href="http://www.thenation.com/article/bernie-sanders-speaks/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.thenation.com/article/bernie-sanders-speaks/', 'The Nation');" target="_blank">
           The Nation
          </a>
          Democratic presidential candidate Sen. Bernie Sanders (I-VT) swears off campaign contributions from the fossil fuel industry  promises to visit red states like Alabama during his campaign  and finally tackles the issue of police brutality.
         </p>
         <p>
          Sanders recalled his long history working on civil rights Igot arrested in trying to desegregate Chicagos school system but was quick to push back on the notion that his campaign has failed to address issues like race relations in favor of more populist economic rhetoric. I do not separate the civil-rights issue from the fact that 50 percent of African-American young people are either unemployed or underemployed. Invoking Dr. Martin Luther King Sanders said The issue that Dr. King raised all the time was: This is great if we want to desegregate restaurants or hotels  but what does it matter if people cant afford to go to them? Thats still the issue today.
         </p>
         <p>
          And the Independent senatorconfronted the stigma surrounding his affiliation as a democratic socialist: Do they think Im afraid of the word? Im not afraid of the word Sanders insisted before ticking off a list of accomplishments in Scandinavian countries like Denmark that have adopted a democratic-socialist approach  including tuition-free college  universal health care and guaranteed paid maternity and paternity leave to argue that
          <a href="http://www.salon.com/2015/07/05/its_bernie_sanders_america_5_radical_ideas_americans_strongly_support/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.salon.com/2015/07/05/its_bernie_sanders_america_5_radical_ideas_americans_strongly_support/', ' most Americans would support such measures');">
           most Americans would support such measures
          </a>
          :
         </p>
         <blockquote>
          <p>
           I happen to believe that if the American people understood the significant accomplishments that have taken place under social-democratic governments  democratic-socialist governments  labor governments throughout Europe  they would be shocked to know about those accomplishments. One of the goals of this campaign is to advance that understanding.
          </p>
          <p>
           (cont..)
          </p>
          <p>
           Source:
           <em>
            <a href="http://www.salon.com/2015/07/06/bernie_sanders_on_why_elites_are_in_for_a_shock_the_discontent_of_the_american_people_is_far_far_greater/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.salon.com/2015/07/06/bernie_sanders_on_why_elites_are_in_for_a_shock_the_discontent_of_the_american_people_is_far_far_greater/', 'Bernie Sanders on why elites are in for a shock: The discontent of the American people is far, far greater  Salon.com');">
             Bernie Sanders on why elites are in for a shock: The discontent of the American people is far, far greater  Salon.com
            </a>
           </em>
          </p>
         </blockquote>
        </blockquote>

      <div class="post-176458 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-health category-international-politicsculture-stuff category-musicentlit tag-artist-draws-under-influence tag-lsd" id="post-176458">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/a-portrait-artist-draws-while-on-lsd-for-science-1950s/" rel="bookmark">
         A portrait artist draws while on LSD for science! (1950s)..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/a-portrait-artist-draws-while-on-lsd-for-science-1950s/" rel="bookmark" title="8:33 pm">
         <span class="entry-date">
          7/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <p>
         <a href="http://boingboing.net/2015/07/06/a-portrait-artist-draws-while.html" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://boingboing.net/2015/07/06/a-portrait-artist-draws-while.html', '');">
          <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://i1.wp.com/boingboing.net/wp-content/uploads/2015/07/vVQD38.gif?resize=480270"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          An artist whose identity has been lost was administered two 50-microgram doses of LSD  each separated by a lapse of one hour and was then asked to draw portraits while under its influence  using the doctor who administered the drugs as a model.
          <span id="more-402501">
          </span>
          It is believed these artworks are part of a study conducted by Oscar Janiger  a University of California-Irvine psychiatrist known for his work on LSD  which started in 1954 and continued on for the next seven years.
         </p>
         <p>
          (cont..)
         </p>
         <p>
          Source:
          <em>
           <a href="http://boingboing.net/2015/07/06/a-portrait-artist-draws-while.html" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://boingboing.net/2015/07/06/a-portrait-artist-draws-while.html', 'A portrait artist draws while on LSD for science! (1950s)  Boing Boing');">
            A portrait artist draws while on LSD for science! (1950s)  Boing Boing
           </a>
          </em>
         </p>
        </blockquote>

             <a class="share-stumbleupon sd-button share-icon" data-shared="" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/a-portrait-artist-draws-while-on-lsd-for-science-1950s/?share=stumbleupon" rel="nofollow" target="_blank" title="Click to share on StumbleUpon">

      <div class="post-176456 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-international-politicsculture-stuff tag-bernie-sanders tag-hillary-clinton" id="post-176456">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/sanders-momentum-in-iowa-leaves-clinton-camp-on-edge/" rel="bookmark">
         Sanders Momentum in Iowa Leaves Clinton Camp on Edge..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/sanders-momentum-in-iowa-leaves-clinton-camp-on-edge/" rel="bookmark" title="4:08 pm">
         <span class="entry-date">
          7/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          Challenging Bernie Sanders directly could elevate his candidacy 
          <a href="http://www.nytimes.com/2015/07/07/us/politics/hillary-clintons-team-is-wary-as-bernie-sanders-finds-footing-in-iowa.html?hp&amp;action=click&amp;pgtype=Homepage&amp;module=photo-spot-region&amp;region=top-news&amp;WT.nav=top-news&amp;_r=1" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.nytimes.com/2015/07/07/us/politics/hillary-clintons-team-is-wary-as-bernie-sanders-finds-footing-in-iowa.html?hp&amp;action=click&amp;pgtype=Homepage&amp;module=photo-spot-region&amp;region=top-news&amp;WT.nav=top-news&amp;_r=1', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://static01.nyt.com/images/2015/07/07/us/07iowajp2/07iowajp2-facebookJumbo-v2.jpg"/>
          </a>
           but the current path requires Hillary Clinton to put faith in caucusgoers who once jilted her.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p class="story-body-text story-content" data-para-count="305" data-total-count="305" id="story-continues-1">
          The ample crowds and unexpectedly strong showing garnered by Senator
          <a href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/2015/05/01/us/elections/bernie-sanders.html?inline=nyt-per" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/2015/05/01/us/elections/bernie-sanders.html?inline=nyt-per', 'Bernie Sanders');" title="More articles about Bernard Sanders.">
           Bernie Sanders
          </a>
          are setting off worry among advisers and allies of
          <a href="http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/2015/04/13/us/elections/hillary-clinton.html?inline=nyt-per" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.nytimes.com/interactive/2015/04/13/us/elections/hillary-clinton.html?inline=nyt-per', 'Hillary Rodham Clinton ');" title="More articles about Hillary Rodham Clinton.">
           Hillary Rodham Clinton 
          </a>
          who believe the Vermont senator could overtake her in Iowa polls by the fall and even defeat her in the nations first nominating contest there.
         </p>
         <p class="story-body-text story-content" data-para-count="469" data-total-count="774">
          The enthusiasm that Mr. Sanders has generated  including a rally attended by 2,500 people in Council Bluffs Iowa  on Friday  has called into question Mrs. Clintons early strategy of focusing on a listening tour of small groups and wooing big donors in private settings.
         </p>
         <p class="story-body-text story-content" data-para-count="251" data-total-count="1025" id="story-continues-2">
          We are worried about him sure. He will be a serious force for the campaign  and I dont think that will diminish Jennifer Palmieri  the Clinton campaigns communications director  said Monday in an interview on MSNBCs Morning Joe.
         </p>
         <p class="story-body-text story-content" data-para-count="251" data-total-count="1276">
          Some of Mrs. Clintons advisers acknowledged that they were surprised by Mr. Sanderss momentum and said there were enough liberal voters in Iowa  including many who supported Barack Obama or John Edwards in 2008  to create problems for her there.
         </p>
         <p class="story-body-text story-content" data-para-count="477" data-total-count="1753">
          I think we underestimated that Sanders would quickly attract so many Democrats in Iowa who werent likely to support Hillary said one Clinton adviser  who like several others spoke on the condition of anonymity to candidly share views about the race. Its too early to change strategy because no one knows if Sanders will be able to hold on to these voters in the months ahead. Were working hard to win them over  but yeah its a real competition there.
         </p>
         <p class="story-body-text story-content" data-para-count="270" data-total-count="2023">
          Asked on Friday about the crowds Mr. Sanders was drawing Mrs. Clinton seemed to walk a careful line with her answer. Well we each run our own campaigns and I always knew this was going to be competitive she told reporters at an ice cream stand in Lebanon, N.H.
         </p>
         <p>
          (cont..)
         </p>
         <p>
          Source:
          <em>
           <a href="http://www.nytimes.com/2015/07/07/us/politics/hillary-clintons-team-is-wary-as-bernie-sanders-finds-footing-in-iowa.html" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.nytimes.com/2015/07/07/us/politics/hillary-clintons-team-is-wary-as-bernie-sanders-finds-footing-in-iowa.html', 'Sanders Momentum in Iowa Leaves Clinton Camp on Edge  The New York Times');">
            Sanders Momentum in Iowa Leaves Clinton Camp on Edge  The New York Times
           </a>
          </em>
         </p>
        </blockquote>

      <div class="post-176453 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-green-things category-health category-international-politicsculture-stuff category-nz-politicsculturestuff category-op-ed category-reviews category-vegan-stuff tag-diet tag-looking-young" id="post-176453">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/people-who-look-younger-really-are-ageing-slower-study-shows-op-ed/" rel="bookmark">
         People who look younger really are ageing slower  study shows.. (+op-ed..)
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/people-who-look-younger-really-are-ageing-slower-study-shows-op-ed/" rel="bookmark" title="11:31 am">
         <span class="entry-date">
          7/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.stuff.co.nz/life-style/life/70017732/people-who-look-younger-really-are-ageing-slower-study-shows" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.stuff.co.nz/life-style/life/70017732/people-who-look-younger-really-are-ageing-slower-study-shows', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://www.stuff.co.nz/content/dam/images/1/5/h/r/x/l/image.related.StuffLandscapeSixteenByNine.620x349.15oq10.png/1436217515042.jpg"/>
          </a>
          NZ study discovers how to track who will stay looking young  and who will appear old before their time.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          Some lucky people look young for their age while others appear old before their time; now researchers from Dunedin can start to tell us why.
         </p>
         <p>
          A method to measure the pace of ageing of people in their 20s or 30s has emerged from the
          <a href="http://www.stuff.co.nz/dominion-post/archive/national-news/128037/Under-the-microscope-from-cradle-to-grave" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.stuff.co.nz/dominion-post/archive/national-news/128037/Under-the-microscope-from-cradle-to-grave', 'University of Otagos long-running Dunedin Multidisciplinary Study');" target="_blank">
           University of Otagos long-running Dunedin Multidisciplinary Study
          </a>
          which has tracked more than 1000 people born in Dunedin in 1972-73 from birth to the present.
         </p>
         <p>
          A large number of health measures such as blood pressure  white blood cell count  liver and kidney function  have been taken regularly along with interviews and other assessments.
         </p>
         <div class="html-asset">
          <div class="twentytwenty-wrapper twentytwenty-horizontal">
           The paper, written by a team from the United States  United Kingdom  Israel  and New Zealand  was published today in the
           <i>
            Proceedings of the National Academy of Sciences
           </i>
          </div>
         </div>
         <p>
          It revealed a panel of 18 biomarkers that could be combined to determine whether people were ageing faster or slower than their peers.
         </p>
         <p>
          When these 18 measures were assessed together in 954 study members at age 38 researchers were able to set biological ages for each person. In contract to chronological ages these ranged from 30 to nearly 60 years.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          (cont..)
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          (ed:..whoar..!..eh..?..all i know is that i know quite a few people who have lived on a vegan diet  for decades  and to a man/woman they both glow with good health and look young for their age..
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          ..from my observations..no booze or ciggies and a healthy vegan dietll do that for ya..eh..?..)
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          Source:
          <em>
           <a href="http://www.stuff.co.nz/life-style/life/70017732/people-who-look-younger-really-are-ageing-slower-study-shows" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.stuff.co.nz/life-style/life/70017732/people-who-look-younger-really-are-ageing-slower-study-shows', 'People who look younger really are ageing slower, study shows | Stuff.co.nz');">
            People who look younger really are ageing slower, study shows | Stuff.co.nz
           </a>
          </em>
         </p>
        </blockquote>

      <div class="post-176451 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-general category-health category-international-politicsculture-stuff category-musicentlit category-nz-politicsculturestuff category-reviews tag-decriminalizing-drugs tag-portugal" id="post-176451">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/greenwald-what-portugal-can-teach-us-about-decriminalizing-drugs/" rel="bookmark">
         Greenwald: What Portugal Can Teach Us About Decriminalizing Drugs..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/greenwald-what-portugal-can-teach-us-about-decriminalizing-drugs/" rel="bookmark" title="10:21 am">
         <span class="entry-date">
          7/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.newsweek.com/greenwald-what-portugal-can-teach-us-about-decriminalizing-drugs-349992" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.newsweek.com/greenwald-what-portugal-can-teach-us-about-decriminalizing-drugs-349992', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/DHbZdgoqRWuVK-GVF6-6W4bS0MzpR5WfKkAMzCdv1fWZ-XKLJzcGUmzsAb6YDS3QedILl9WdAeJ0pWWfJd7QFCSbRtYHEDR4HMTga3l_yCVf5BcWN4L0Lo5HhXpsF7MgagRKa0A"/>
          </a>
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          None of the scenarios touted by opponentsrampant increases in drug use by the young; Lisbon becoming a drug tourist havenhas occurred.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p class="hs-text-container" dir="ltr">
          On July 1 2001 a nationwide law in Portugal took effect that decriminalized all drugs including cocaine and heroin.
         </p>
         <p dir="ltr">
          Under the new legal framework all drugs were decriminalized not legalized. Thus drug possession for personal use and drug usage itself are still legally prohibited but violations of those prohibitions are deemed to be exclusively administrative violations and are removed completely from the criminal realm. Drug trafficking continues to be prosecuted as a criminal offense.
         </p>
         <p dir="ltr">
          While other states in the European Union have developed various forms of de facto decriminalizationwhereby substances perceived to be less serious (such as cannabis) rarely lead to criminal prosecutionPortugal remains the only EU member state with a law explicitly declaring drugs to be decriminalized. Because more than seven years have now elapsed since enactment of Portugals decriminalization system there are ample data enabling its effects to be assessed.
         </p>
         <p dir="ltr">
          Notably, decriminalization has become increasingly popular in Portugal since 2001. Except for some far-right politicians very few domestic political factions are agitating for a repeal of the 2001 law. And while there is a widespread perception that bureaucratic changes need to be made to Portugals decriminalization framework to make it more efficient and effective there is no real debate about whether drugs should once again be criminalized.
         </p>
         <p dir="ltr">
          More significantly none of the nightmare scenarios touted by preenactment decriminalization opponents  from rampant increases in drug usage among the young to the transformation of Lisbon into a haven for drug tourists has occurred.
         </p>
         <p>
          (cont..)
         </p>
         <p>
          Source:
          <em>
           <a href="http://www.newsweek.com/greenwald-what-portugal-can-teach-us-about-decriminalizing-drugs-349992" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.newsweek.com/greenwald-what-portugal-can-teach-us-about-decriminalizing-drugs-349992', 'Greenwald: What Portugal Can Teach Us About Decriminalizing Drugs');">
            Greenwald: What Portugal Can Teach Us About Decriminalizing Drugs
           </a>
          </em>
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <div class="sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled">
         <div class="robots-nocontent sd-block sd-social sd-social-icon-text sd-sharing">

      <div class="post-176438 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-international-politicsculture-stuff tag-greece tag-yanis-varoufakis" id="post-176438">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/the-greek-blokes-resigned-hes-run-rings-round-em/" rel="bookmark">
         The Greek blokes resigned. Hes run rings round em..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/the-greek-blokes-resigned-hes-run-rings-round-em/" rel="bookmark" title="9:12 am">
         <span class="entry-date">
          7/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2015/jul/06/yanis-varoufakis-resigned-greek-crisis" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/world/2015/jul/06/yanis-varoufakis-resigned-greek-crisis', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://static.guim.co.uk/sys-images/Guardian/Pix/pictures/2015/7/6/1436185791434/732d1902-d544-466d-870a-4fe4bb34ebf4-1020x612.jpeg"/>
          </a>
          UK analyst predicts Yanis Varoufakiss departure may help in Greek crisis talks but as the City will admit no one really knows what will occur next.
          <br/>
          The Greek blokes resigned. Hes run rings round em.
         </p>
         <p>
          Those words were how one City trader was overheard explaining the resignation of Greek finance minister
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="auto-linked-tag" data-link-name="auto-linked-tag" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/yanis-varoufakis" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/world/yanis-varoufakis', 'Yanis Varoufakis');">
           Yanis Varoufakis
          </a>
           as he chatted on the phone in early trading  following the Greek referendum.
         </p>
         <p>
          It represented what was a brief hum of excitement in the City as the markets opened on Monday morning  for the first time since the Hellenic Republic voted no. Like eurozone officials the Square Mile had been expecting that last weeks taster of capital controls would spook the country into a yes vote in the countrys austerity referendum and financial spread-betting firm IG Group last week priced a no vote as having only a 40% chance.
         </p>
         <p>
          So what now? Monday mornings initial dips in the value of the euro and the worlds stock markets have been swiftly reversed  the euro is now down less than 1% against the dollar  while the FTSE is off by even less  as investors quickly started to buy again in the hope of a deal.
         </p>
         <p>
          (cont..)
         </p>
         <p>
          Source:
          <em>
           <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2015/jul/06/yanis-varoufakis-resigned-greek-crisis" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/world/2015/jul/06/yanis-varoufakis-resigned-greek-crisis', 'The Greek blokes resigned. Hes run rings round em | World news | The Guardian');">
            The Greek blokes resigned. Hes run rings round em | World news | The Guardian
           </a>
          </em>
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <div class="sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled">
         <div class="robots-nocontent sd-block sd-social sd-social-icon-text sd-sharing">

      <!-- #post-## -->
      <div class="post-176435 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-general category-green-things category-health category-international-politicsculture-stuff category-nz-politicsculturestuff category-op-ed category-vegan-stuff tag-health tag-inequality tag-op-ed" id="post-176435">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/healthcare-heals-the-sick-better-pay-keeps-them-healthy-in-the-first-place-op-ed/" rel="bookmark">
         Healthcare heals the sick. Better pay keeps them healthy in the first place.. (+ op-ed..)
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/healthcare-heals-the-sick-better-pay-keeps-them-healthy-in-the-first-place-op-ed/" rel="bookmark" title="8:38 am">
         <span class="entry-date">
          7/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2015/jul/06/health-care-pay-equity-environment" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2015/jul/06/health-care-pay-equity-environment', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://media.guim.co.uk/5749c366439120fa33dde095091dd0589b50accb/0_211_5121_3073/master/5121.jpg"/>
          </a>
          Broader insurance access is great  but its more effective to prevent people from getting sick  and socioeconomic equality helps do that.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          While Obamacare has expanded access to insurance (and thus to care)  available estimates and evidence indicate that increasing the numbers of insured Americans will only marginally impact either health or health spending.
          <br/>
          The answers actually lie in socioeconomic and environmental policies that affect how people live and work  the real drivers of individual and collective well-being. These issues  generally outside the purview of health policy must become central to it and their impacts on health and healthcare spending should be routinely evaluated.
         </p>
         <div class="js-ad-slot ad-slot ad-slot--dfp ad-slot--inline1 ad-slot--inline" data-link-name="ad slot inline1" data-mobile="1,1|300,50|300,250" data-mobile-landscape="1,1|300,50|320,50|300,250" data-name="inline1" data-node-uid="6" data-tablet="1,1|300,250" data-test-id="ad-slot-inline1" id="dfp-ad--inline1">
          <div class="ad-slot__label" data-test-id="ad-slot-label">
           Social  economic  psychological  behavioral and environmental risk factors for health are quite unequally distributed in America. Disadvantaged socioeconomic groups and racial and ethnic minorities have greater exposure to and experience of almost all risk factors. And these disparities are generally getting larger. For some disadvantaged areas and people life expectancy is actually
           <a class=" u-underline" data-component="in-body-link" data-link-name="in body link" href="http://content.healthaffairs.org/content/31/8/1803.abstract?sid=473f4d31-4fab-41c6-8c36-7661da8669f0" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://content.healthaffairs.org/content/31/8/1803.abstract?sid=473f4d31-4fab-41c6-8c36-7661da8669f0', 'declining ');">
            declining 
           </a>
           something largely without precedent in our  or any  wealthy nation. The greatest opportunity for making Americans healthier lies in improving access to education  income and better occupational and residential conditions.
          </div>
         </div>
         <p>
          Reducing toxic and dangerous environmental exposures for example  has improved health in hazardous occupations and polluted communities. Policies to reduce cigarette smoking have arguably been the single biggest source of health improvements over the last half century. Both observational and experimental evidence
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="in-body-link" data-link-name="in body link" href="http://muse.jhu.edu/books/9781610444873" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://muse.jhu.edu/books/9781610444873', 'show');">
           show
          </a>
          that policies that increase education and income  from early childhood education to Pell grants to Social Security  improve the health of both children and adults. Better education and income facilitate people having safer and healthier jobs  schools  homes  neighborhoods  behaviors and lifestyles and utilizing more cost-effective health services  such as regular primary care rather than emergency rooms.
         </p>
         <p>
          Implementing such policies will help our countrys financial bottom line. Healthy people and nations have lower healthcare use and spending; sick people and nations spend more.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          (cont:..)
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          (ed:..and with our rampant inequality/poverty (with all the now known outcomes/downline-costs) we are most definitely a sick nation..
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          how can we not be..?..
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          ..and the real shame is that we also have a sick labour party  one so dedicated to preserving the status quo..(labour election 14 policy: benefit-levels to only rise at rate of inflation)..
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          ..that they seem unable to see/do what needs to be done  to make new zealand not sick  but healthy..)
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <p>
         Source:
         <em>
          <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2015/jul/06/health-care-pay-equity-environment" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2015/jul/06/health-care-pay-equity-environment', 'Healthcare heals the sick. Better pay keeps them healthy in the first place | James House | Comment is free | The Guardian');">
           Healthcare heals the sick. Better pay keeps them healthy in the first place | James House | Comment is free | The Guardian
          </a>
         </em>
        </p>

      <div class="post-176433 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-general category-international-politicsculture-stuff category-nz-politicsculturestuff tag-capitalism tag-tech" id="post-176433">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/when-we-blame-tech-for-everything-capitalism-gets-off-the-hook/" rel="bookmark">
         When we blame tech for everything  capitalism gets off the hook..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/when-we-blame-tech-for-everything-capitalism-gets-off-the-hook/" rel="bookmark" title="8:13 am">
         <span class="entry-date">
          7/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2015/jul/06/blame-technology-capitalism-smartphones" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2015/jul/06/blame-technology-capitalism-smartphones', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://static.guim.co.uk/sys-images/Guardian/Pix/pictures/2015/7/5/1436113655760/A-businessman-checking-hi-009.jpg"/>
          </a>
          Our smartphones and computers make us permanently contactable and on-call. But we should be angry at capitalist structures  not app developers.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          When it comes to looking for things to blame as we evaluate the current state of society though  were missing something critical. The problem is not tech: its capitalism. Admitting the real source of the problem creates an opportunity to address it. Capitalism has adroitly managed to evade responsibility and neatly slip its leash but we should be able to exercise greater critical thinking than that and bring it to heel. Capitalism and tech are deeply intertwined of course  but lets not confuse the two.
         </p>
         <p>
          Were constantly enmeshed in our devices because we have to be. Most of us work in professions with an unreasonable expectation of employees  believing that we should be available at all times to perform all labour. Thats been facilitated by tech  which makes it easier to contact people  but tech shouldnt shoulder all the blame. Its capitalism that took advantage of this opportunity to work it  turning it into something that could be used to control employees and keep them constantly within arms reach.
         </p>
         <p>
          The person who refuses to be constantly available or who exercises discretion in terms of the kind of work performed after hours wont last long at a company and certainly wont advance in terms of salary and rank.
         </p>
         <div class="js-ad-slot ad-slot ad-slot--dfp ad-slot--inline1 ad-slot--inline" data-link-name="ad slot inline1" data-mobile="1,1|300,50|300,250" data-mobile-landscape="1,1|300,50|320,50|300,250" data-name="inline1" data-node-uid="14" data-tablet="1,1|300,250" data-test-id="ad-slot-inline1" id="dfp-ad--inline1">
          <div class="ad-slot__label" data-test-id="ad-slot-label">
           Tech feeds into capitalism  and capitalism feeds into tech.
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="ad-slot__label" data-test-id="ad-slot-label">
         </div>
         <div class="ad-slot__label" data-test-id="ad-slot-label">
          (cont..)
         </div>
         <div class="ad-slot__label" data-test-id="ad-slot-label">
         </div>
         <div class="ad-slot__label" data-test-id="ad-slot-label">
          Source:
          <em>
           <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2015/jul/06/blame-technology-capitalism-smartphones" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2015/jul/06/blame-technology-capitalism-smartphones', 'When we blame tech for everything, capitalism gets off the hook | SE Smith | Comment is free | The Guardian');">
            When we blame tech for everything, capitalism gets off the hook | SE Smith | Comment is free | The Guardian
           </a>
          </em>
         </div>
        </blockquote>
        <div class="sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled">

      <div class="post-176430 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-general category-international-politicsculture-stuff category-op-ed tag-democracy tag-greece" id="post-176430">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/greeces-fight-is-for-democracy-in-europe-thats-why-we-must-support-it-op-ed/" rel="bookmark">
         Greeces fight is for democracy in Europe. Thats why we must support it..(+ op-ed..)
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/greeces-fight-is-for-democracy-in-europe-thats-why-we-must-support-it-op-ed/" rel="bookmark" title="7:55 am">
         <span class="entry-date">
          7/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2015/jul/06/greece-democracy-europe-eu" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2015/jul/06/greece-democracy-europe-eu', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://static.guim.co.uk/sys-images/Guardian/Pix/pictures/2015/7/6/1436184403490/1432b8f6-c59c-46ea-a0cb-9da3c926468b-2060x1236.jpeg"/>
          </a>
          The EU powers told Greeks their world would cave in unless they acquiesced by voting yes. The no vote has raised the political stakes even higher.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <div class="content__meta-container js-content-meta js-football-meta u-cf&lt;/p&gt;&lt;br /&gt; &lt;p&gt; content__meta-container--tonal-header&lt;/p&gt;&lt;br /&gt; &lt;p&gt; ">
          <span class="drop-cap drop-cap--wide">
           <span class="drop-cap__inner">
            F
           </span>
          </span>
          rom the cradle of democracy,
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="in-body-link" data-link-name="in body link" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/live/2015/jul/06/greek-referendum-eu-leaders-call-crisis-meeting-as-bailout-rejected-live-updates" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/world/live/2015/jul/06/greek-referendum-eu-leaders-call-crisis-meeting-as-bailout-rejected-live-updates', 'a lion has roared');" title="">
           a lion has roared
          </a>
          . It is difficult to overstate the pressure the Greek people have
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="in-body-link" data-link-name="in body link" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/video/2015/jul/06/greek-greece-referendum-reactions-syntagma-no-oxi-vote-videeo" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/world/video/2015/jul/06/greek-greece-referendum-reactions-syntagma-no-oxi-vote-videeo', 'both endured and defied');" title="">
           both endured and defied
          </a>
          . A country that has already experienced an austerity-induced economic disaster with few precedents among developed nations in peacetime has suffered a sustained campaign of economic and political warfare. The European Central Bank  which has
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="in-body-link" data-link-name="in body link" href="http://www.ft.com/cms/s/0/e705d260-0e82-11e4-b1c4-00144feabdc0.html#axzz3f6mkWbC6" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.ft.com/cms/s/0/e705d260-0e82-11e4-b1c4-00144feabdc0.html#axzz3f6mkWbC6', 'only recently deigned to publish some of the minutes of its meetings');" title="">
           only recently deigned to publish some of the minutes of its meetings
          </a>
           capped liquidity for Greek banks  driving them to the verge of collapse. There were stringent capital controls and desperate queues outside banks followed. A country desperate to stay within the euro was told it would be ejected and with calamitous results.Martin Schulz  the European parliaments president and a so-called social democrat  whose attitude towards democracy can be generously described as ambiguous  called for the removal of Greeces elected government in favour of a technocratic government.
         </div>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          It wasnt bluster. Thats what the EU and the markets previously pulled off in Greece and yes in Italy: however much justifiable distaste exists for Silvio Berlusconi it should have been his own people who removed him.
         </p>
         <p>
          In
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="auto-linked-tag" data-link-name="auto-linked-tag" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/greece" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/world/greece', 'Greece');">
           Greece
          </a>
          itself the oligarch-owned free media acted as a political machine (sound familiar?) -pumping out relentless propaganda in favour of capitulating to the creditors demands. An alliance between Greeces economic elite and the EU great powers told the Greek people: however tough your lives have been in the last few years your world will cave in unless you acquiesce. And still the Greek people voted no  not narrowly but overwhelmingly.
         </p>
         <p>
          (cont..)
         </p>
         <p>
          (ed:..also interesting here in nz how the neoliberal/austerity-pimping media (to a man/woman) are in a chorus of shock/horror at the perfidy of those greeks..how dare hey..!..they splutter thru their thin-lips/furrowed brows..as they drench the media with racist-diatribes..blaming the greek lack of character for what their past government did..(the equivalent here would be blaming all new zealanders for muldoon cancelling that super scheme (on ideological-grounds..and has any political bad-decision cost us more..?..)
         </p>
         <p>
          .and what i am hoping comes out from all of this is that the likes of the nz labour party see the overwhelming support there can be from a people bowed by poverty/austerity for policies that actually help most of the people  and not just the elites/corporate-world..the banks..
         </p>
         <p>
          ..and that they grow a set of balls..so as to take advantage of the political-lessons proffered to them by the greek people..)
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          Source:
          <em>
           <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2015/jul/06/greece-democracy-europe-eu" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2015/jul/06/greece-democracy-europe-eu', 'Greeces fight is for democracy in Europe. Thats why we must support it | Owen Jones | Comment is free | The Guardian');">
            Greeces fight is for democracy in Europe. Thats why we must support it | Owen Jones | Comment is free | The Guardian
           </a>
          </em>
         </p>
        </blockquote>

            <li class="share-end">
            </li>
           </ul>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
