      <div class="post-176427 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-general category-international-politicsculture-stuff category-musicentlit category-nz-politicsculturestuff category-op-ed category-reviews tag-beatles tag-john-lennon tag-paul-mccartney" id="post-176427">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/lennonmccartney-songwriting-credit-why-paul-wont-let-it-be-op-ed/" rel="bookmark">
         Lennon/McCartney songwriting credit: why Paul wont let it be..(+ op-ed..)
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/lennonmccartney-songwriting-credit-why-paul-wont-let-it-be-op-ed/" rel="bookmark" title="7:20 am">
         <span class="entry-date">
          7/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/music/shortcuts/2015/jul/06/mccartney-lennon-paul-songwriting-credit-beatles" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/music/shortcuts/2015/jul/06/mccartney-lennon-paul-songwriting-credit-beatles', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://static.guim.co.uk/sys-images/Guardian/Pix/pictures/2015/7/6/1436200846718/adb1ec46-b5ee-4be9-b508-c98cb9e9158f-2060x1236.jpeg"/>
          </a>
          The former Beatle has once again vented his frustrations at taking second billing on songs he wrote. Cant they just come together?
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <div class="content__meta-container js-content-meta js-football-meta u-cf&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt; content__meta-container--no-byline&lt;/p&gt;&lt;br /&gt; &lt;p&gt; ">
          <strong>
           Age:
          </strong>
          around 58 years
         </div>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Appearance:
          </strong>
          increasingly miffed.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           What have
           <a class=" u-underline" data-component="auto-linked-tag" data-link-name="auto-linked-tag" href="http://www.theguardian.com/music/paulmccartney" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/music/paulmccartney', 'Paul McCartney');">
            Paul McCartney
           </a>
           and John Lennon got to be miffed about? Only one of them is still alive.
          </strong>
          You mean Lennon and McCartney  thats the way the songwriting Beatles are always credited.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Alphabetically? Seems fair.
          </strong>
          True  but Macca is unhappy about taking second billing on songs he wrote.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Oh, let it be.
          </strong>
          Exactly. That was a song to which Lennon contributed nothing, but which still gets attributed to Lennon/McCartney. Worse  in the digital age  in some online lists you get Lennon  and no McCartney.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           This bird has flown.
          </strong>
          Maybe, but in an interview in
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="in-body-link" data-link-name="in body link" href="http://www.esquire.co.uk/culture/music/8511/paul-mccartney-interview/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.esquire.co.uk/culture/music/8511/paul-mccartney-interview/', 'this months Esquire magazine');">
           this months Esquire magazine
          </a>
          , he complains not just about coming second on the credit but that the canonisation of Lennon after his murder in 1980 reduced his own creative roles to the margins. I understood that now there was going to be revisionism he says. It was going to be: John was the one.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Nowhere man?
          </strong>
          Thats the way Paul feels.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Jealous guy.
          </strong>
          Thats how the Lennonists see it.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           We can work it out.
          </strong>
          I hope so.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           All you need is love.
          </strong>
          Quite.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           All things must pass.
          </strong>
          Actually that one was written by George. Even so  it doesnt look as if McCartney will be backing down any time soon.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          (cont..)
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          (ed:..sheesh paul..!..maybe you need a good strong joint..eh..?..to chill out..you are sounding like a moaning bitter old man..and yes you banged out some good ditties..but john was the thinking/political one..wasnt he..?
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          (nb:..mccartney claims he has given up on the herb..he needs to rethink that stance..)
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          Source:
          <em>
           <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/music/shortcuts/2015/jul/06/mccartney-lennon-paul-songwriting-credit-beatles" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/music/shortcuts/2015/jul/06/mccartney-lennon-paul-songwriting-credit-beatles', 'Lennon/McCartney songwriting credit: why Paul wont let it be | Music | The Guardian');">
            Lennon/McCartney songwriting credit: why Paul wont let it be | Music | The Guardian
           </a>
          </em>
         </p>
        </blockquote>

      <div class="post-176425 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-general category-international-politicsculture-stuff category-musicentlit category-reviews tag-animal-cruelty tag-religious-rituals tag-spain" id="post-176425">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/were-a-violent-nation-director-tackles-spains-festival-culture-of-animal-cruelty/" rel="bookmark">
         Were a violent nation  director tackles Spains festival culture of animal cruelty..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/were-a-violent-nation-director-tackles-spains-festival-culture-of-animal-cruelty/" rel="bookmark" title="7:00 am">
         <span class="entry-date">
          7/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2015/jul/06/violent-nation-spain-festival-animal-cruelty-turkey-bulls-film-santa-fiesta" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/world/2015/jul/06/violent-nation-spain-festival-animal-cruelty-turkey-bulls-film-santa-fiesta', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://i.guim.co.uk/static/w-640/h-360/q-95/sys-images/Guardian/Pix/audio/video/2015/6/12/1434119194560/KP_272578_crop_640x360.jpg"/>
          </a>
          As tens of thousands flock to Pamplona for the annual running of the bulls  Miguel ngel Rolland explains why he made his documentary Santa Fiesta.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          It hurts me to say it but the Spanish are a savage insensitive and ignorant people says Miguel ngel Rolland. In his new documentary, the Spanish film-maker has chronicled some of the 16,000 religious festivals across
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="auto-linked-tag" data-link-name="auto-linked-tag" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/spain" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/world/spain', 'Spain');">
           Spain
          </a>
          that he says involve the torture of animals.
         </p>
         <p>
          Every year about 60,000 animals are killed during these festivals  often held in honour of a local saint or the Virgin Mary. Spanish identity is a local rather than a national affair and people are fiercely loyal to their town or village and the customs associated with it.
         </p>
         <p>
          The best known festival is this weeks running of the bulls during the fiesta of San Fermn in Pamplona. Tens of thousands of people from all over the world flock to the small Navarra town each year for a week of partying that begins each day with six fighting bulls and six oxen being driven through the narrow streets to the bullring  where the bulls are killed in a series of bullfights.
         </p>
         <p>
          The festival has attracted increasing criticism from animal rights groups  on Saturday activists from Peta staged a protest to draw attention to what they say is a week of fear and death for bulls.
         </p>
         <p>
          The cruelties documented in
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="in-body-link" data-link-name="in body link" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/video/2015/jul/06/animal-abuse-film-spanish-festivals-video-santa-fiesta" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/world/video/2015/jul/06/animal-abuse-film-spanish-festivals-video-santa-fiesta', 'Rollands film');">
           Rollands film
          </a>
          (warning: graphic scenes) include pulling the head off a goose and throwing a live turkey from a church tower  but the most abused animal by far is the bull.
         </p>
         <p>
          (cont..)
         </p>
         <p>
          Source:
          <em>
           <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2015/jul/06/violent-nation-spain-festival-animal-cruelty-turkey-bulls-film-santa-fiesta" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/world/2015/jul/06/violent-nation-spain-festival-animal-cruelty-turkey-bulls-film-santa-fiesta', 'Were a violent nation  director tackles Spains festival culture of animal cruelty | World news | The Guardian');">
            Were a violent nation  director tackles Spains festival culture of animal cruelty | World news | The Guardian
           </a>
          </em>
         </p>
        </blockquote>

      <div class="post-176423 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-general" id="post-176423">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/should-i-go-vegan-to-lose-weight/" rel="bookmark">
         Should I go vegan to lose weight?..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/should-i-go-vegan-to-lose-weight/" rel="bookmark" title="6:16 am">
         <span class="entry-date">
          7/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/lifeandstyle/2015/jul/06/should-i-go-vegan-to-lose-weight-diet-vegetarian" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/lifeandstyle/2015/jul/06/should-i-go-vegan-to-lose-weight-diet-vegetarian', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://static.guim.co.uk/sys-images/Guardian/Pix/pictures/2015/7/3/1435933964817/Should-I-go-vegan-009.jpg"/>
          </a>
          Veganism can reduce risk of some health problems and recent research showed that dieters who cut out meat  eggs and dairy lost more weight than others.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <span class="drop-cap drop-cap--wide">
           <span class="drop-cap__inner">
            T
           </span>
          </span>
          here can only be one thing worse than trying to squeeze yourself into a swimming costume and thats being a vegan. No meat eggs or diary  nothing that comes from animals. Is there anything interesting left to eat? Yes theres lots  according to vegans  including chickpeas  kidney beans  fortified soy products  fruit and nuts. So this weeks research linking vegan diet and weight loss is a triumph for the tofu burger. Vegetarian diets have previously been linked with a reduced risk of Type 2 diabetes  heart disease and dying from pretty much everything. But more importantly  at least as far as summer magazine issues go  vegan diets havent been strongly linked with weight loss. This is partly because studies on weight loss and varities of vegetarianism have been small  lasted varying amounts of time and the subjects studied havent stuck to their diets.
         </p>
         <h2>
          <strong>
           The solution
          </strong>
         </h2>
         <p>
          This new study, a meta analysis published in the
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="in-body-link" data-link-name="in body link" href="http://link.springer.com/article/10.1007%2Fs11606-015-3390-7" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://link.springer.com/article/10.1007%2Fs11606-015-3390-7', 'Journal of General Internal Medicine');" title="">
           Journal of General Internal Medicine
          </a>
          , adds up the results of the best studies that compare weight loss in vegetarian and non-vegetarian diets- and also lacto-ovo vegetarians (who drink milk and eat eggs) and vegans. The studies included 1,151 dieters who had followed a regime for between nine and 74 weeks. The diets included the Atkins diet and those recommended by the
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="in-body-link" data-link-name="in body link" href="http://www.diabetes.org/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.diabetes.org/', 'American Diabetes Association');" title="">
           American Diabetes Association
          </a>
          and the
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="in-body-link" data-link-name="in body link" href="http://www.nhlbi.nih.gov/health-pro/guidelines/current/cholesterol-guidelines/final-report" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.nhlbi.nih.gov/health-pro/guidelines/current/cholesterol-guidelines/final-report', 'USNational Cholesterol Education Program');" title="">
           USNational Cholesterol Education Program
          </a>
          .
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          Those who followed a vegetarian diet lost an average of 1.48kg more than those on other diets  while vegans lost 2.52kg more than the non-vegetarian dieters.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          (cont..)
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          Source:
          <em>
           <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/lifeandstyle/2015/jul/06/should-i-go-vegan-to-lose-weight-diet-vegetarian" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/lifeandstyle/2015/jul/06/should-i-go-vegan-to-lose-weight-diet-vegetarian', 'Should I go vegan to lose weight? | Life and style | The Guardian');">
            Should I go vegan to lose weight? | Life and style | The Guardian
           </a>
          </em>
         </p>
        </blockquote>

      <div class="post-176421 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-international-politicsculture-stuff tag-greece" id="post-176421">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/yanis-varoufakis-angela-merkel-has-a-red-and-a-yellow-button-one-ends-the-crisis-which-does-she-push/" rel="bookmark">
         Yanis Varoufakis: Angela Merkel has a red and a yellow button. One ends the crisis. Which does she push?..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/yanis-varoufakis-angela-merkel-has-a-red-and-a-yellow-button-one-ends-the-crisis-which-does-she-push/" rel="bookmark" title="6:02 am">
         <span class="entry-date">
          7/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2015/jul/06/yanis-varoufakis-angela-merkel-crisis-global-minotaur-capitalism-europe" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2015/jul/06/yanis-varoufakis-angela-merkel-crisis-global-minotaur-capitalism-europe', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://i.guim.co.uk/img/media/59a5a0bafe62f78e9b14b60ce82392f00d4d9e0d/0_0_3765_2258/master/3765.jpg?w=620&amp;q=85&amp;auto=format&amp;sharp=10&amp;s=8f3493209fa2c7da4023908470e87a96"/>
          </a>
          The Global Minotaur of neoliberal capitalism centred on Wall Street held the world to ransom from 1971 to 2008. Now Europes surplus countries are trying to prop up its corpse.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          In the past two years the debate in Europe has focused exclusively on issues that sound technical and minor: will there be 
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="in-body-link" data-link-name="in body link" href="http://www.e-ir.info/2013/11/01/eu-conditionality-an-effective-means-for-policy-reform/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.e-ir.info/2013/11/01/eu-conditionality-an-effective-means-for-policy-reform/', 'conditionality');" title="">
           conditionality
          </a>
           attached to the purchases of Italian and Spanish bonds by the European Central Bank? Will the ECB supervise all of Europes banks or just the 
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="in-body-link" data-link-name="in body link" href="http://www.eba.europa.eu/risk-analysis-and-data/global-systemically-important-institutions" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.eba.europa.eu/risk-analysis-and-data/global-systemically-important-institutions', 'systemic');" title="">
           systemic
          </a>
           ones?
         </p>
         <p>
          These are questions that ought to be of no genuine interest to anyone other than those with a morbid interest in the interface between public finance and monetary policy. And yet these questions (and the manner in which they will be answered) will probably prove as important for the future of Europe as the treaties of
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="in-body-link" data-link-name="in body link" href="http://www.historytoday.com/richard-cavendish/treaty-westphalia" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.historytoday.com/richard-cavendish/treaty-westphalia', 'Westphalia');" title="">
           Westphalia
          </a>
          ,
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="in-body-link" data-link-name="in body link" href="http://www.history.co.uk/study-topics/history-of-ww2/treaty-of-versailles" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.history.co.uk/study-topics/history-of-ww2/treaty-of-versailles', 'Versailles');" title="">
           Versailles
          </a>
          or even
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="in-body-link" data-link-name="in body link" href="http://www.civitas.org.uk/eufacts/FSTREAT/TR1.php" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.civitas.org.uk/eufacts/FSTREAT/TR1.php', 'Rome');" title="">
           Rome
          </a>
          . For these are the issues that will determine whether Europe holds together or succumbs to the vicious centrifugal forces that were unleashed by the crash of 2008.
         </p>
         <p>
          Even so they are not issues that are worth expounding upon here. All they do is to reflect a tragic underlying reality that can be described in simple lay terms without the use of any jargon whatsoever:
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="auto-linked-tag" data-link-name="auto-linked-tag" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/europe-news" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/world/europe-news', 'Europe');">
           Europe
          </a>
          is disintegrating because its architecture was simply not sound enough to sustain the shockwaves caused by the death throes of what I call the Global Minotaur: the system of neoliberal capitalism centred on Wall Street  extracting tribute from the world after 1971.
         </p>
         <p>
          (cont..)
         </p>
         <p>
          Source:
          <em>
           <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2015/jul/06/yanis-varoufakis-angela-merkel-crisis-global-minotaur-capitalism-europe" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2015/jul/06/yanis-varoufakis-angela-merkel-crisis-global-minotaur-capitalism-europe', 'Yanis Varoufakis: Angela Merkel has a red and a yellow button. One ends the crisis. Which does she push? | Comment is free | The Guardian');">
            Yanis Varoufakis: Angela Merkel has a red and a yellow button. One ends the crisis. Which does she push? | Comment is free | The Guardian
           </a>
          </em>
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <div class="sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled">
         <div class="robots-nocontent sd-block sd-social sd-social-icon-text sd-sharing">

      <div class="post-176419 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-international-politicsculture-stuff tag-bernie-sanders tag-five-policies" id="post-176419">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/its-bernie-sanders-america-5-radical-ideas-americans-strongly-support/" rel="bookmark">
         Its Bernie Sanders America: 5 radical ideas Americans strongly support..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/its-bernie-sanders-america-5-radical-ideas-americans-strongly-support/" rel="bookmark" title="5:44 pm">
         <span class="entry-date">
          6/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.salon.com/2015/07/05/its_bernie_sanders_america_5_radical_ideas_americans_strongly_support/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.salon.com/2015/07/05/its_bernie_sanders_america_5_radical_ideas_americans_strongly_support/', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://media.salon.com/2015/07/bernie_sanders10.jpg"/>
          </a>
          Think the democratic socialist is a fringe candidate? You may be surprised how many Americans agree with him.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p dir="ltr">
          <strong>
           Taxing The Rich
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p dir="ltr">
          Sanders called the massive transfer of wealth from the middle class to the top one-tenth of 1 percent in America obscene and has called for a return to a much higher marginal tax rate. If you have seen a massive transfer of wealth from the middle class to the top tenth of 1 percent youve got to transfer that back Sanders told
          <a href="http://www.cnbc.com/id/102694365" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.cnbc.com/id/102694365', 'CNBC');">
           CNBC
          </a>
          .
         </p>
         <p dir="ltr">
          And Sanders lists Americas top 10 corporate tax avoiders on his
          <a href="http://www.sanders.senate.gov/top-10-corporate-tax-avoiders" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.sanders.senate.gov/top-10-corporate-tax-avoiders', 'Senate website');">
           Senate website
          </a>
          and details thecompensation packages of Americas wealthiest CEOs.
         </p>
         <p dir="ltr">
          Sixty-four percent of Americans say they are bothered a lot by the feeling that some corporations arent paying whats fair in federal taxes and 61 percent say the same about some wealthy people  according to a recent
          <a href="http://www.people-press.org/2015/03/19/federal-tax-system-seen-in-need-of-overhaul/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.people-press.org/2015/03/19/federal-tax-system-seen-in-need-of-overhaul/', 'Pew poll');">
           Pew poll
          </a>
          . Meanwhile 67 percent of Americans
          <a href="http://www.gallup.com/poll/166904/dissatisfied-income-wealth-distribution.aspx" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.gallup.com/poll/166904/dissatisfied-income-wealth-distribution.aspx', 'recently told Gallup');">
           recently told Gallup
          </a>
          they were dissatisfied with the way income and wealth are distributed in the U.S.
         </p>
         <p>
          (cont..)
         </p>
         <p>
          Source:
          <em>
           <a href="http://www.salon.com/2015/07/05/its_bernie_sanders_america_radical_ideas_americans_strongly_support/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.salon.com/2015/07/05/its_bernie_sanders_america_radical_ideas_americans_strongly_support/', 'Its Bernie Sanders America: 5 radical ideas Americans strongly support  Salon.com');">
            Its Bernie Sanders America: 5 radical ideas Americans strongly support  Salon.com
           </a>
          </em>
         </p>
        </blockquote>

      <div class="post-176417 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-health category-international-politicsculture-stuff category-nz-politicsculturestuff tag-cancer tag-meat" id="post-176417">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/like-meat-and-beer-hate-cancer/" rel="bookmark">
         Like Meat and Beer?  Hate Cancer?..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/like-meat-and-beer-hate-cancer/" rel="bookmark" title="4:36 pm">
         <span class="entry-date">
          6/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.motherjones.com/blue-marble/2014/03/science-says-beer-marinade-could-prevent-cancer" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.motherjones.com/blue-marble/2014/03/science-says-beer-marinade-could-prevent-cancer', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://www.motherjones.com/files/beerbecue.jpg"/>
          </a>
          Spring is coming.Before long, beer-drinking men and women will be coaxing fiery embers to life and tossing dead animals onto charred metal grates above them. Ahh the sizzle and snap of fat as it hits red hot coals. Oh no! Whats that you say? Carcinogens are caused by the c
          <a href="http://pubs.acs.org/doi/abs/10.1021/jf404966w" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://pubs.acs.org/doi/abs/10.1021/jf404966w', 'ontact of dripping fat with hot embers');" target="_blank">
           ontact of dripping fat with hot embers
          </a>
          ?
         </p>
         <p>
          Fear not eager human. And keep a couple of your dark winter beers handy  because researchers from Portugal and Spain have found that marinating your pork chops in dark beer dramatically reduces carcinogenic contamination. Rejoice!
         </p>
         <p>
          Smoke  pyrolysis (organic matter decomposing in intense heat)  and dripping fat can all cause the accumulation of polycyclic aromatic hydrocarbons (PAHs) on charcoal-grilled meats. According to the
          <a href="http://www.epa.gov/osw/hazard/wastemin/minimize/factshts/pahs.pdf" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.epa.gov/osw/hazard/wastemin/minimize/factshts/pahs.pdf', 'EPA');" target="_blank">
           EPA
          </a>
          , PAHs have caused tumors  birth defects and reproductive problems in lab animalsthough the Agency clarifies that these effects have not yet been observed in humans.
         </p>
         <p>
          You can also find PAHs in cigarette smoke and car exhaust.
         </p>
         <p>
          (cont..)
         </p>
         <p>
          Source:
          <em>
           <a href="http://www.motherjones.com/blue-marble/2014/03/science-says-beer-marinade-could-prevent-cancer" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.motherjones.com/blue-marble/2014/03/science-says-beer-marinade-could-prevent-cancer', 'Like Meat and Beer? Hate Cancer? | Mother Jones');">
            Like Meat and Beer? Hate Cancer? | Mother Jones
           </a>
          </em>
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <div class="sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled">

      <div class="post-176411 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-international-politicsculture-stuff tag-osborne tag-welfare-reform" id="post-176411">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/osborne-to-cap-family-benefits/" rel="bookmark">
         Osborne to cap family benefits..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/osborne-to-cap-family-benefits/" rel="bookmark" title="11:49 am">
         <span class="entry-date">
          6/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.independent.co.uk/news/uk/home-news/osborne-to-cap-family-benefits-at-23000--announced-ahead-of-his-postelection-budget-10366862.html" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.independent.co.uk/news/uk/home-news/osborne-to-cap-family-benefits-at-23000--announced-ahead-of-his-postelection-budget-10366862.html', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://www.independent.co.uk/incoming/article10366311.ece/alternates/w460/41-George-Osborne-Get.jpg"/>
          </a>
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          The amount of benefits that can be claimed by one family in a year will be cut below 23,000 inside London  George Osborne announced today.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          The Chancellor said he has identified 12bn of welfare cuts and vowed to create a welfare system that is fair not just to those who need it but to those who pay for it.
         </p>
         <p>
          He confirmed his Budget would cut tax credits  which top up low incomes. He said they cost a couple of billion pounds a year when introduced by Gordon Brown in the nineties but now cost 30bn.
         </p>
         <p>
          Mr Osborne reacted coolly to growing pressure by Tories for him to urge employers to pay the Living Wage  which is higher than the national minimum wage. He insisted the best way to boost earnings was to reduce taxes on working people adding that was the straightforward, Conservative way of doing this.
         </p>
         <p>
          (cont..)
         </p>
         <p>
          Source:
          <em>
           <a href="http://www.independent.co.uk/news/uk/home-news/osborne-to-cap-family-benefits-at-23000--announced-ahead-of-his-postelection-budget-10366862.html" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.independent.co.uk/news/uk/home-news/osborne-to-cap-family-benefits-at-23000--announced-ahead-of-his-postelection-budget-10366862.html', 'Osborne to cap family benefits at 23,000  announced ahead of his post-election Budget  Home News  UK  The Independent');">
            Osborne to cap family benefits at 23,000  announced ahead of his post-election Budget  Home News  UK  The Independent
           </a>
          </em>
         </p>
        </blockquote>

      <div class="post-176409 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-international-politicsculture-stuff tag-eu tag-greece" id="post-176409">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/greece-referendum-reaction-eu-mulls-next-steps-as-vote-threatens-biggest-crisis-in-its-history/" rel="bookmark">
         Greece referendum reaction: EU mulls next steps as vote threatens biggest crisis in its history..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/greece-referendum-reaction-eu-mulls-next-steps-as-vote-threatens-biggest-crisis-in-its-history/" rel="bookmark" title="11:21 am">
         <span class="entry-date">
          6/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/europe/greece-referendum-live-reaction-eu-mulls-next-steps-as-vote-threatens-biggest-crisis-in-its-history-10367616.html" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/europe/greece-referendum-live-reaction-eu-mulls-next-steps-as-vote-threatens-biggest-crisis-in-its-history-10367616.html', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://www.independent.co.uk/incoming/article10365036.ece/alternates/w1024/8-Yes-No-Greece-AFP.jpg"/>
          </a>
          The European Union held out the chance of a fresh dialogue with Athens in the wake of crushing victory of the Greek government in Sundays referendum on a bailout package  with officials in Brussels and elsewhere indicating they were still willing to discuss new bailout terms.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <div class="widget storyContent article widget-editable viziwyg-section-1024 inpage-widget-8939454 articleContent">
          <p>
           German Chancellor Angela Merkel is due to meet French President Francois Hollande in Paris on Monday night to discuss the situation  with sources suggesting an emergency EU summit could be held in Brussels on Wednesday. Already there are reports that Greek Prime Minister Alexis Tsipras had spoken with several European leaders  including Mr Hollande and European Central Bank (ECB) president Mario Draghi.
          </p>
         </div>
         <p>
          Martin Schulz  the European Parliaments president  said the eurozone summit on Tuesday should consider an immediate humanitarian aid programme for Greece.
         </p>
         <p>
          He blamed the Greek government for the current crisis but said ordinary people should not suffer as a result.
         </p>
         <p>
          Mr Schulz urged Athens to make meaningful and constructive proposals in talks with the other eurozone countries. If not we are entering a very difficult and even dramatic time he said.
         </p>
         <p>
          (cont..)
         </p>
         <p>
          Source:
          <em>
           <a href="http://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/europe/greece-referendum-live-reaction-eu-mulls-next-steps-as-vote-threatens-biggest-crisis-in-its-history-10367616.html" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/europe/greece-referendum-live-reaction-eu-mulls-next-steps-as-vote-threatens-biggest-crisis-in-its-history-10367616.html', 'Greece referendum reaction: EU mulls next steps as vote threatens biggest crisis in its history  Europe  World  The Independent');">
            Greece referendum reaction: EU mulls next steps as vote threatens biggest crisis in its history  Europe  World  The Independent
           </a>
          </em>
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <div class="sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled">

      <div class="post-176403 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-general category-green-things category-international-politicsculture-stuff category-musicentlit category-nz-politicsculturestuff category-reviews tag-cyborgs tag-sapiens" id="post-176403">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/the-age-of-the-cyborg-has-begun-and-the-consequences-cannot-be-known/" rel="bookmark">
         The age of the cyborg has begun  and the consequences cannot be known..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/the-age-of-the-cyborg-has-begun-and-the-consequences-cannot-be-known/" rel="bookmark" title="8:26 am">
         <span class="entry-date">
          6/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/culture/2015/jul/05/yuval-harari-sapiens-interview-age-of-cyborgs" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/culture/2015/jul/05/yuval-harari-sapiens-interview-age-of-cyborgs', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://static.guim.co.uk/sys-images/Observer/Pix/pictures/2015/7/1/1435754467436/Yuval-Harari-author-of-Sa-009.jpg"/>
          </a>
          The author of the bestselling Sapiens says that the future of life on Earth is now  worryingly  in the hands of a very small group of entrepreneurs.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          And his book is a brilliant read. He zips from subject to subject  through thousands of years of human history  alighting on whatever seems to take his fancy but gradually builds up a picture of us as well as what exactly? As more successful monkeys basically  so successful that weve enslaved all the other animals and bent the planet to our will. But whereas sharks and lions evolved over millennia to take their place at the top of the food chain  Harari compares us to banana republic dictators who just got here. They came to power very violently and lately so they feel extremely insecure about their position. So all the time they just take more and more power to beef up their position.
         </p>
         <figure class="element element-image img--landscape fig--narrow-caption fig--has-shares" data-media-id="d7d5cf2742588c978a44b39a631e1083f906789c" id="img-2">
          <a class="article__img-container js-gallerythumbs" data-is-ajax="" data-link-name="Launch Article Lightbox" href="http://www.theguardian.com/culture/2015/jul/05/yuval-harari-sapiens-interview-age-of-cyborgs#img-2" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/culture/2015/jul/05/yuval-harari-sapiens-interview-age-of-cyborgs#img-2', '');">
           <img alt="A chimpanzee alpha male would never think of using his power in order to go on holiday into the territory of a neighbouring chimpanzee band." class="gu-image" src="http://i.guim.co.uk/img/static/sys-images/Guardian/Pix/pictures/2015/7/2/1435840932162/f8a800f5-53d5-4835-ad39-db116e0755a4-1020x612.jpeg?w=620&amp;q=85&amp;auto=format&amp;sharp=10&amp;s=b3829a4f17c7ac9d853d5dbb201fc91b"/>
          </a>
          <figcaption class="caption caption--img caption caption--img">
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          Because in Hararis view we have no real idea what we want even at the most basic personal level  let alone as a species. Even what people take to be their most personal desires are usually programmed by the imagined order. Theres nothing natural or obvious about taking a holiday abroad he says  by way of example. A chimpanzee alpha male would never think of using his power in order to go on holiday into the territory of a neighbouring chimpanzee band. The elite of ancient Egypt spent their futures building pyramids and having their corpses mummified but none of them thought of going shopping in Babylon. Were all victims of the myths of romantic consumerism he says.
         </p>
         <p>
          (cont..)
         </p>
         <p>
          Source:
          <em>
           <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/culture/2015/jul/05/yuval-harari-sapiens-interview-age-of-cyborgs" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/culture/2015/jul/05/yuval-harari-sapiens-interview-age-of-cyborgs', 'Yuval Noah Harari: The age of the cyborg has begun  and the consequences cannot be known | Culture | The Guardian');">
            Yuval Noah Harari: The age of the cyborg has begun  and the consequences cannot be known | Culture | The Guardian
           </a>
          </em>
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <div class="sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled">
         <div class="robots-nocontent sd-block sd-social sd-social-icon-text sd-sharing">

      <!-- #post-## -->
      <div class="post-176400 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-general category-international-politicsculture-stuff tag-dogs" id="post-176400">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/throwaway-pup-trend-makes-britons-dogs-worst-enemies/" rel="bookmark">
         Throwaway pup trend makes Britons dogs worst enemies..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/throwaway-pup-trend-makes-britons-dogs-worst-enemies/" rel="bookmark" title="8:09 am">
         <span class="entry-date">
          6/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2015/jul/05/throwaway-puppies-marc-abraham-dog-lovers" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/world/2015/jul/05/throwaway-puppies-marc-abraham-dog-lovers', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://static.guim.co.uk/sys-images/Observer/Pix/pictures/2015/7/4/1436003561415/TV-vet-Marc-Abraham-exami-009.jpg"/>
          </a>
          Fickle owners  poor training and battery farms  threaten UK reputation as nation of dog lovers.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <div class="content__meta-container js-content-meta js-football-meta u-cf&lt;/p&gt;&lt;br /&gt; &lt;p&gt; ">
          Britain risks losing its standing as a nation of dog lovers thanks to a new and appalling trend in throwaway puppies  according to charities. TV vet  author and animal welfare campaigner
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="in-body-link" data-link-name="in body link" href="http://www.marcthevet.com/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.marcthevet.com/', 'Marc Abraham');" title="">
           Marc Abraham
          </a>
          said impulse buying of dogs  fuelled by unscrupulous internet dealers and bad practices in puppy farming  is leading to a rapid rise in cruelty cases while legislation to protect animals is a total mess.
         </div>
         <p>
          Were getting worse as a nation of supposed animal lovers. Puppies are so easy to get hold of that they have become disposable. You can just dump them when you have had enough and rescue centres up and down the country are bursting at the seams. We have seen a massive increase in demand for whatever breed is fashionable  whether its a husky from
          <em>
           Twilight
          </em>
          or
          <em>
           Game of Thrones 
          </em>
          or Lady Gaga and YouTubers like
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="in-body-link" data-link-name="in body link" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=__dtoZ0UzlI" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=__dtoZ0UzlI', 'DanTDM');" title="">
           DanTDM
          </a>
          with their French bulldogs and pugs. They see a cute dog on
          <em>
           EastEnders 
          </em>
          google it  find out they can order one and have it delivered the next day.
         </p>
         <p>
          Such hapless owners have no idea how to train or socialise their dogs and end up selling them on or dumping them he said. Mistreatment and poor care and diet leave dogs with behavioural problems and rescue centres then struggle to find new homes for them. So we have this huge demand that the breeders cant cope with  rescue centres overwhelmed and these big battery farms spewing out more said Abraham  who has set up
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="in-body-link" data-link-name="in body link" href="http://pupaid.org/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://pupaid.org/', 'PupAid ');" title="">
           PupAid 
          </a>
          a campaign for better controls and licensing in the puppy trade.
         </p>
         <p>
          (cont..)
         </p>
         <p>
          Source:
          <em>
           <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/2015/jul/05/throwaway-puppies-marc-abraham-dog-lovers" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/world/2015/jul/05/throwaway-puppies-marc-abraham-dog-lovers', 'Throwaway pup trend makes Britons dogs worst enemies | World news | The Guardian');">
            Throwaway pup trend makes Britons dogs worst enemies | World news | The Guardian
           </a>
          </em>
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <div class="sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled">

      <div class="post-176397 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-green-things category-international-politicsculture-stuff category-nz-politicsculturestuff tag-heathrow-5th-runway" id="post-176397">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/its-too-late-to-save-our-world-so-enjoy-the-spectacle-of-doom/" rel="bookmark">
         Its too late to save our world  so enjoy the spectacle of doom
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/its-too-late-to-save-our-world-so-enjoy-the-spectacle-of-doom/" rel="bookmark" title="7:40 am">
         <span class="entry-date">
          6/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2015/jul/05/too-late-to-save-world-heathrow-runway-stewart-lee" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2015/jul/05/too-late-to-save-world-heathrow-runway-stewart-lee', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://static.guim.co.uk/sys-images/Guardian/Pix/pictures/2015/7/3/1435924694081/922c56b6-8219-43ac-aebc-e580e67d4b1c-2060x1236.jpeg"/>
          </a>
          The business world is right  lets just get on with the third Heathrow runway  and the extinction of all life on Earth while were at it  why delay the inevitable?
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          In the middle of a week of record temperatures  as if unaware of the irony  the business community celebrated the consolidation of its attempts to force the governments hand to agree to a third filth-generating runway at
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="auto-linked-tag" data-link-name="auto-linked-tag" href="http://www.theguardian.com/travel/heathrow" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/travel/heathrow', 'Heathrow ');">
           Heathrow 
          </a>
          tipping all species on Earth towards extinction. Everything will die soon  except for cockroaches  and Glastonbury favourite the Fall  who will survive even a nuclear holocaust though they will still refuse to play their 80s chart hits.In Norfolk on Thursday the tarmac melted and
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="in-body-link" data-link-name="in body link" href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-england-norfolk-33371515" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-england-norfolk-33371515', 'ducklings became trapped in sticky blackness');" title="">
           ducklings became trapped in sticky blackness
          </a>
          . When a lioness whelped in an ancient Roman street Caesar thought something was up. Here solid matter transmuted to hot liquid and swallowed baby birds whole. How surreal do the signs and warnings have to become before we stop in our tracks? Are whales required to fall from the sky? Does Tim Henman have to give birth to a two-headed cat on Centre Court?
         </p>
         <p>
          CBI director John Cridland says: The government must commit to the decision now  and get diggers in the ground at Heathrow swiftly by 2020. Head of the Institute of Directors Simon Walker says: There can now be no further delay from politicians. And Segro chief executive David Sleath merely bellows: Get on with it! like some selfish
          <em>
           Top Gear
          </em>
          presenter demanding his steak dinner after dawdling  the planet itself the powerless BBC employee he punchesin the face.
         </p>
         <aside class="element element-rich-link element--thumbnail element-rich-link--upgraded" data-component="rich-link" data-link-name="rich-link-1 | 1">
          <div class="rich-link tone-editorial--item ">
           <div class="rich-link__container">
            <div class="rich-link__read-more-text">
             The business community has thrown its executive toys out of the pram  and now there are chrome ball bearings on strings everywhere  tripping up unpaid interns and making life difficult for immigrant cleaners scrabbling under desks on less than minimum wage. David Cameron  an electoral promise to oppose the third runway sticking in his throat like an undigested salmon bone  can only duck his cowardly head and hope some terrible atrocity or a Wimbledon win wafts our attention away.
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="rich-link__read-more-text">
          </div>
          <div class="rich-link__read-more-text">
          </div>
          <div class="rich-link__read-more-text">
           (cont..)
          </div>
          <div class="rich-link__read-more-text">
          </div>
          <div class="rich-link__read-more-text">
          </div>
          <div class="rich-link__read-more-text">
           Source:
           <em>
            <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2015/jul/05/too-late-to-save-world-heathrow-runway-stewart-lee" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2015/jul/05/too-late-to-save-world-heathrow-runway-stewart-lee', 'Its too late to save our world, so enjoy the spectacle of doom | Stewart Lee | Comment is free | The Guardian');">
             Its too late to save our world, so enjoy the spectacle of doom | Stewart Lee | Comment is free | The Guardian
            </a>
           </em>
          </div>
         </aside>
        </blockquote>

      <!-- #post-## -->
      <div class="post-176392 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-international-politicsculture-stuff tag-greece-referendum-result" id="post-176392">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/greece-heads-towards-historic-no-vote-against-austerity-measures/" rel="bookmark">
         Greece heads towards historic no vote against austerity measures..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/greece-heads-towards-historic-no-vote-against-austerity-measures/" rel="bookmark" title="6:39 am">
         <span class="entry-date">
          6/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/business/2015/jul/05/greece-referendum-early-results-historic-no-vote-against-austerity" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/business/2015/jul/05/greece-referendum-early-results-historic-no-vote-against-austerity', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://i.guim.co.uk/static/w-640/h-360/q-95/sys-images/Guardian/Pix/audio/video/2015/7/5/1436103862456/KP_343677_crop_640x360.jpg"/>
          </a>
          With more than 30% of the results counted official projection from Greeces interior ministry shows no vote set to win with an overwhelming 61% share.
          <br/>
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="auto-linked-tag" data-link-name="auto-linked-tag" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/greece" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/world/greece', 'Greece');">
           Greece
          </a>
          is on the brink of a historic no vote against the austerity measures demanded by its international creditors  according to the first results.
         </p>
         <p>
          Two hours after the polls closed and with more 30% of the results counted the official opinion polls showed the no camp on over 60% and the yes camp with about 40%. An official projection from Greeces interior ministry showed the no votes set to win with an overwhelming 61% share of the vote.
         </p>
         <p>
          If the final result reflects these early figures it could risk plunging
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="auto-linked-tag" data-link-name="auto-linked-tag" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/europe-news" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/world/europe-news', 'Europe');">
           Europe
          </a>
          deeper into crisis and would send shockwaves across global financial markets.
         </p>
         <p>
          While the ballot papers were still being counted polls conducted by telephone were showing knife-edge results  but all were pointing towards the no vote that the prime minister
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="auto-linked-tag" data-link-name="auto-linked-tag" href="http://www.theguardian.com/world/alexis-tsipras" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/world/alexis-tsipras', 'Alexis Tsipras');">
           Alexis Tsipras
          </a>
          had asked for.
         </p>
         <figure class="element element-image img--landscape fig--narrow-caption fig--has-shares" data-media-id="25816eabf79e01d383e7d7e8e0454d23c4d37f67" id="img-1">
          <a class="article__img-container js-gallerythumbs" data-is-ajax="" data-link-name="Launch Article Lightbox" href="http://www.theguardian.com/business/2015/jul/05/greece-referendum-early-results-historic-no-vote-against-austerity#img-1" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/business/2015/jul/05/greece-referendum-early-results-historic-no-vote-against-austerity#img-1', '');">
           <img alt="An anti-austerity voter celebrates the as early results showed the no vote inching ahead." class="gu-image" src="http://i.guim.co.uk/img/media/25816eabf79e01d383e7d7e8e0454d23c4d37f67/0_198_5028_3018/master/5028.jpg?w=620&amp;q=85&amp;auto=format&amp;sharp=10&amp;s=058820f4f5afdbf3df8322c82d85ccfe"/>
          </a>
          <figcaption class="caption caption--img caption caption--img">
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          His government has insisted that a no vote will not mean an end to negotiations with the International Monetary Fund  the European Union and the
          <a class=" u-underline" data-component="auto-linked-tag" data-link-name="auto-linked-tag" href="http://www.theguardian.com/business/european-central-bank" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/business/european-central-bank', 'European Central Bank');">
           European Central Bank
          </a>
           over a package of reforms to enable Greece to resume payments to its creditors and reopen its banks.
         </p>
         <p>
          (cont..)
         </p>
         <p>
          Source:
          <em>
           <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/business/2015/jul/05/greece-referendum-early-results-historic-no-vote-against-austerity" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/business/2015/jul/05/greece-referendum-early-results-historic-no-vote-against-austerity', 'Greece heads towards historic no vote against austerity measures | Business | The Guardian');">
            Greece heads towards historic no vote against austerity measures | Business | The Guardian
           </a>
          </em>
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <div class="sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled">
         <div class="robots-nocontent sd-block sd-social sd-social-icon-text sd-sharing">

      <div class="post-176390 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-international-politicsculture-stuff category-musicentlit tag-free-maijuana tag-weed-the-people" id="post-176390">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/free-pot-for-2000-folks-at-oregons-weed-the-people-event/" rel="bookmark">
         Free pot for 2,000 folks at Oregons Weed the People event..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/free-pot-for-2000-folks-at-oregons-weed-the-people-event/" rel="bookmark" title="3:56 pm">
         <span class="entry-date">
          5/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <p>
         <a href="http://boingboing.net/2015/07/04/free-pot-for-2000-folks-at-or.html" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://boingboing.net/2015/07/04/free-pot-for-2000-folks-at-or.html', '');">
          <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://media.boingboing.net/wp-content/uploads/2015/07/5500914557_e1cf9722f7_b.jpg"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         Although recreational marijuana is legal to grow and smoke in Oregon its not yet legal to sell. But that doesnt mean you cant give it away to 2,000 people  which is what Portlands Weed the People event did yesterday. The first festival of its kind in the U.S. people 21 and over were able
         <a href="http://www.theguardian.com/us-news/2015/jul/04/oregon-marijuana-laws-weed-the-people" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.theguardian.com/us-news/2015/jul/04/oregon-marijuana-laws-weed-the-people', 'to spend the day sampling free weed and everything weed-related');">
          to spend the day sampling free weed and everything weed-related
         </a>
         .
        </p>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          The alcohol-free event lasted for seven hours  as attendees mulled around to test out smoking devices- relaxed on comfy chairs and listened to records in a chill out area and waited in a line that wound through the inside of a warehouse to enter the Grow Garden the highly secured and roped off area where they could pick up their free goodies.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <p>
         The historic event was put on by growers and medical marijuana dispensaries (who can sell in Oregon to people with medical cards)- and tickets to enter were $40.
        </p>
        <p>
         (cont..)
        </p>
        <p>
         Source:
         <em>
          <a href="http://boingboing.net/2015/07/04/free-pot-for-2000-folks-at-or.html" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://boingboing.net/2015/07/04/free-pot-for-2000-folks-at-or.html', 'Free pot for 2,000 folks at Oregons Weed the People event  Boing Boing');">
           Free pot for 2,000 folks at Oregons Weed the People event  Boing Boing
          </a>
         </em>
        </p>

      <div class="post-176386 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-international-politicsculture-stuff category-musicentlit category-nz-politicsculturestuff category-reviews tag-einstein" id="post-176386">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/albert-einstein-the-humanitarian-2/" rel="bookmark">
         Albert Einstein  the Humanitarian..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/albert-einstein-the-humanitarian-2/" rel="bookmark" title="3:27 pm">
         <span class="entry-date">
          5/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.utne.com/science-and-technology/albert-einstein-humanitarian-ze0z1404zcalt.aspx" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.utne.com/science-and-technology/albert-einstein-humanitarian-ze0z1404zcalt.aspx', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://www.utne.com/~/media/Images/UTR/Editorial/Articles/Online%20Articles/2014/04-01/Albert%20Einstein%20the%20Humanitarian/Albert-Einstein%20jpg.jpg"/>
          </a>
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          Along with his renowned scientific accomplishments Albert Einstein should be acknowledged for his humanitarian struggles to achieve peace and international cooperation.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <h2>
          Einsteins Cosmic Religion
         </h2>
         <h2>
         </h2>
         <p>
          Einsteins idea of religion  rather than fashioned by dogma dictated  prescribed  and refashioned over the ages by millions of self-appointed experts and unquestioning believers  is based on a more constant themethat of nature and her almost unwavering, harmonious laws. 
         </p>
         <p>
          I believe in Spinozas God  who reveals himself in the lawful harmony of the world  not in a God who concerns himself with the fate and the doings of mankind. In this way Einstein was unifying science and religion and referred to himself as a deeply religious nonbeliever. Moreover being open-minded and inclusive in his worldview  he found Jesus  Buddha  and Moses equally compelling as prophets.
         </p>
         <p>
          (cont..)
         </p>
         <p>
          Source:
          <em>
           <a href="http://www.utne.com/science-and-technology/albert-einstein-humanitarian-ze0z1404zcalt.aspx" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.utne.com/science-and-technology/albert-einstein-humanitarian-ze0z1404zcalt.aspx', 'Albert Einstein, the Humanitarian  Science and Technology  Utne Reader');">
            Albert Einstein, the Humanitarian  Science and Technology  Utne Reader
           </a>
          </em>
         </p>
        </blockquote>

      <div class="post-176382 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-general category-international-politicsculture-stuff tag-bernie-sanders" id="post-176382">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/the-real-reasons-bernie-sanders-is-transforming-the-election-heres-why-he-galvanizes-the-left/" rel="bookmark">
         The real reasons Bernie Sanders is transforming the election: Heres why he galvanizes the left..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/the-real-reasons-bernie-sanders-is-transforming-the-election-heres-why-he-galvanizes-the-left/" rel="bookmark" title="11:03 am">
         <span class="entry-date">
          5/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.salon.com/2015/07/03/the_real_reasons_bernie_sanders_is_transforming_the_election_heres_why_he_galvanizes_the_left/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.salon.com/2015/07/03/the_real_reasons_bernie_sanders_is_transforming_the_election_heres_why_he_galvanizes_the_left/', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://media.salon.com/2015/05/bernie_sanders7.jpg"/>
          </a>
          With Bernie Sanders, its leadership on the issues  not a cult of personality  propelling his long-shot bid.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p dir="ltr">
          CNN dubbed this 
          <a href="http://www.cnn.com/2015/06/26/politics/hillary-clinton-summer-of-bernie-sanders/index.html" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.cnn.com/2015/06/26/politics/hillary-clinton-summer-of-bernie-sanders/index.html', 'the summer of Sanders');" target="_blank">
           the summer of Sanders
          </a>
          as media outlets finally picked up on the large crowds Independent Vermont Senator Bernie Sanders has attracted during campaign stops. His rocketing poll numbers in early primary states like Iowa and New Hampshire led to countless stories heralding a Sanders surge  but the story is as much about the issues as it is about the man.
         </p>
         <p dir="ltr">
          Even Republican candidates have taken notice of Sanders rise. Ahead of a recent stop in Madison  Wisconsin  likely 2016 contender and Wisconsin Governor Scott Walker welcomed Sanders to the state with a
          <a href="http://www.salon.com/2015/07/02/bernie_sanders_is_for_real_new_poll_shows_him_chipping_away_at_hillarys_lead_in_iowa/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.salon.com/2015/07/02/bernie_sanders_is_for_real_new_poll_shows_him_chipping_away_at_hillarys_lead_in_iowa/', 'series of tweets');">
           series of tweets
          </a>
          attacking the democratic socialist once dismissed as too fringe. Walker may not have taken too fondly to Sanders attracting a record 10,000 people in his home state.
         </p>
         <p dir="ltr">
          But Sanders campaign  surely more so than that of any of the Republican candidates  seems to be gaining traction more for the ideas he espouses than because of a cult of personality.
         </p>
         <p dir="ltr">
          Granted  many supporters have pointed to Sanders straightforward manner and willingness to call out bad actors as refreshingly appealing  but unlike with Republican presidential candidates Donald Trump and Chris Christie  it isnt just a brash style thats being sold. Sanders makes a direct effort to address many of the issues that have arisen since the Hope &amp; Change campaign of 2008 and it appears as though he is tapping into very real and long-simmering sentiments in the Democratic base.
         </p>
         <p dir="ltr">
          More than a protest vote against Hillary Clinton  as some have suggested  Sanders support appears to be support for issues Clintons yet to fully address. Here are some of the ways that Sanders is gaining support by leading on issues or movements that other candidates ignore:
         </p>
         <p>
          (cont..)
         </p>
         <p>
          Source:
          <em>
           <a href="http://www.salon.com/2015/07/03/the_real_reasons_bernie_sanders_is_transforming_the_election_heres_why_he_galvanizes_the_left/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.salon.com/2015/07/03/the_real_reasons_bernie_sanders_is_transforming_the_election_heres_why_he_galvanizes_the_left/', 'The real reasons Bernie Sanders is transforming the election: Heres why he galvanizes the left  Salon.com');">
            The real reasons Bernie Sanders is transforming the election: Heres why he galvanizes the left  Salon.com
           </a>
          </em>
         </p>
        </blockquote>

      <div class="post-176380 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-international-politicsculture-stuff category-musicentlit category-reviews tag-grateful-dead" id="post-176380">
       <h2 class="entry-title">
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/i-wont-see-the-end-of-the-year-backstage-at-jerry-garcia-and-the-grateful-deads-final-shows/" rel="bookmark">
         I wont see the end of the year': Backstage at Jerry Garcia and the Grateful Deads final shows..
        </a>
       </h2>
       <div class="entry-meta">
        <span class="meta-prep meta-prep-author">
         Posted on
        </span>
        <a href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/2015/i-wont-see-the-end-of-the-year-backstage-at-jerry-garcia-and-the-grateful-deads-final-shows/" rel="bookmark" title="9:56 am">
         <span class="entry-date">
          5/7/2015
         </span>
        </a>
        <span class="meta-sep">
         by
        </span>
        <span class="author vcard">
         <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.whoar.co.nz/author/phil-ure/" title="View all posts by Phil">
          Phil
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <!-- .entry-meta -->
       <div class="entry-content">
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.salon.com/2015/07/04/i_wont_see_the_end_of_the_year_backstage_at_jerry_garcia_and_the_grateful_deads_final_shows/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.salon.com/2015/07/04/i_wont_see_the_end_of_the_year_backstage_at_jerry_garcia_and_the_grateful_deads_final_shows/', '');">
           <img alt="" class="alignnone size-full" src="http://media.salon.com/2015/07/jerry_garcia.jpg"/>
          </a>
          The Grateful Dead were exhausted in spring 95  Garcia most of all. Heres the bands story of those last days.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          Three songs into the show  the house lights still on  the time had come for Dire Wolf but with a perverse twist no one had anticipated. Twenty-five years had passed since the Dead had recorded that song at Pacific High studio. Theyd played it innumerable times since  occasionally slowing it down a half step. But tonight in the middle of Indiana they again injected it with the crisp merry gait of the recorded version and even the songs refrain harked back to its original impending-death inspiration. Please, dont murder me Jerry Garcia sang again- now in a voice weathered by age and abuse  as cops pivoted their heads  hoping to catch sight of the man whod vowed to kill Garcia before the night was over.
         </p>
         <p>
          Along with the likes of Alpine Valley Music Theatre in Wisconsin the Deer Creek Music Center had become a destination spot  a revered haven  for the Dead and their fans alike. Springing up amid cornfields and cow pastures a half-hour north of Indianapolis the amphitheater was like the band an enclave unto itself. Out there the straight world never felt so distant.
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          (cont..)
         </p>
        </blockquote>
        <blockquote>
         <p>
          Source:
          <em>
           <a href="http://www.salon.com/2015/07/04/i_wont_see_the_end_of_the_year_backstage_at_jerry_garcia_and_the_grateful_deads_final_shows/" onclick="__gaTracker('send', 'event', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.salon.com/2015/07/04/i_wont_see_the_end_of_the_year_backstage_at_jerry_garcia_and_the_grateful_deads_final_shows/', 'I wont see the end of the year: Backstage at Jerry Garcia and the Grateful Deads final shows  Salon.com');">
            I wont see the end of the year: Backstage at Jerry Garcia and the Grateful Deads final shows  Salon.com
           </a>
          </em>
         </p>
        </blockquote>
